18|9|Do you think that the people of the Cave and the Inscription were of Our only wondrous signs
18|10|When the youths took refuge in the Cave, and said, “Our Lord, grant us mercy from Yourself, and show us the right way in our ordeal.”
18|11|Then We caused them to fall into a deep sleep in the cave for many years
18|12|Then We awakened them so that We may see which of the two parties would be more precise in calculating the length of their stay
18|13|We relate to you their story in truth. They were youths who believed in their Lord, and We gave them more guidance
18|14|We strengthened their hearts when they stood up and proclaimed, “Our Lord is the Lord of the heavens and earth. We will never call upon any god other than Him, or we would be uttering an outrageous lie.”
18|15|These people of ours have taken besides Him other gods. Why do they not bring a clear proof about them? Who does greater wrong than one who fabricates lies against Allah
18|16|When you have distanced yourselves from them and what they worship other than Allah, take refuge in the cave; your Lord will extend His mercy to you and make for you an easy way out of your ordeal.”
18|17|You would have seen the sun when it rose, it would incline away from their Cave to the right; and when it set, it would turn away from them to the left, while they were in its open space. That was one of the signs of Allah. Whoever Allah guides is rightly guided, and whoever He causes to stray, you will never find for him a protecting guide
18|18|You would have thought they were awake, although they were asleep. We turned them over on their right and left sides, while their dog stretching its forelegs at the entrance. If you had seen them, you would have fled away from them, filled with horror
18|19|Similarly, We awakened them so that they might question one another. One of them said, “How long have you been here?” They said, “We have been here for a day or part of a day.” They said, “Your Lord knows best how long have you been here. Send one of you with these silver coins of yours to the city, and let him see who has the most pure food and bring some provision from it. And be cautious and let no one know about you
18|20|For if they find out about you, they will stone you or force you back to their religion, and then you will never succeed.”
18|21|This is how We made their case known so that the people might know that the promise of Allah is true and that there is no doubt about the Hour, when they were disputing among themselves concerning their matter [of resurrection], they said, “Build a structure over them. Their Lord knows best about them.” Those who prevailed in their matter said, “We will surely build over them a place of worship.”
18|22|Some will say, “They were three, their dog was the fourth,” while others will say, “They were five, their dog was the sixth,” – merely guessing at the unseen. And others will say, “They were seven, their dog was the eighth.” Say, “My Lord knows best their number; no one knows about them except a few. So do not argue about them except in a brief manner, nor ask anyone about them.”
18|23|And never say about anything, “I will surely do this tomorrow,”
18|24|without adding, “if Allah wills.” And remember your Lord if you forget, and say, “My Lord will hopefully guide me to something closer to what is right.”
18|25|They remained in their cave for three hundred years, plus nine
18|26|Say, “Allah knows best how long they remained. To Him belongs [knowledge of] the unseen of the heavens and earth. How well He sees and how well He hears! They have no protector besides Him, and He shares His command with none.”
18|27|Recite what has been revealed to you from the Book of your Lord. None can change His Words, and you will never find any refuge except with Him
18|28|Be patient with those who call upon their Lord morning and evening, seeking His pleasure. Do not turn your eyes away from them, desiring the adornments of the life of this world. And do not obey one whose heart We have made heedless of Our remembrance, who follows his desires and whose affair is at loss
18|29|Say, “The truth is from your Lord. Whoever wills may believe, and whoever wills may disbelieve.” We have prepared for the wrongdoers a Fire which will encompass them like the walls. If they cry for relief, they will be relieved with water like boiling oil that will scald the faces. What a terrible drink, and what a terrible resting place
18|30|Those who believe and do righteous deeds, We will not let the reward of those who do good deeds to be lost
18|31|It is they who will have Gardens of Eternity, under which rivers flow. They will be adorned therein with golden bracelets and will wear green garments of fine silk and brocade, reclining on adorned couches. What an excellent reward, and what a pleasant resting place
18|32|Give them an example of two men: to one of them We gave two gardens of grapevines and surrounded them with palm trees, and placed between them crops
18|33|Each garden yielded its produce and did not fall short in the least, and We caused a stream to flow through them
18|34|And he had abundant fruit. He said to his companion, as he was conversing with him, “I am greater than you in wealth and superior in following.”
18|35|He entered his garden, having wronged himself, and said, “I do not think that this will ever perish
18|36|nor do I think that the Hour will ever come. Even if I am brought back to my Lord, I will surely find something better than this.”
18|37|His companion said, while conversing with him, “Do you disbelieve in He Who created you from dust, then from a sperm-drop, then fashioned you into a well proportioned man
18|38|As for me: He is Allah, my Lord, and I do not associate anyone with my Lord
18|39|If only you had said, when you entered your garden, ‘This is by Allah’s Will; there is no power except with Allah.’ Even though you see me inferior to you in wealth and children
18|40|it may well be that my Lord will give me something better than your garden, and send upon your garden a thunderbolt from the heaven, turning it into a barren land
18|41|Or its water may sink, so you will never be able to get it back.”
18|42|Eventually all his produce was destroyed and he started wringing his hands [in dismay] over what he had spent on it, as it had collapsed on its trellises, and he said, “Oh, would that I had not associated anyone with my Lord!”
18|43|He had none to support him against Allah, nor could he support himself
18|44|In that situation, the authority only rests with Allah, the True God. He is best in reward and best in outcome
18|45|Give them the example of the life of this world: it is like the plants of the earth, thriving when sustained by the rain We send down from the sky, but soon they turn into chaff scattered by the winds. Allah has full power over all things
18|46|Wealth and children are the adornment of the life of this world, but the lasting righteous deeds are better with your Lord in reward and better in hope
18|47|And [beware of] the Day when We will move the mountains away, and you will see the earth laid bare; We will gather them all and not leave behind anyone of them
18|48|They will be presented before your Lord in rows, “Now you have come to Us as We created you the first time, although you claimed that We would never appoint a time for your return.”
18|49|And the record [of deeds] will be placed before them, and you will see the wicked scared of what it contains. They will say, “Woe to us! What is this book that leaves nothing, small or big, except that it has recorded it?” They will find all what they did before them, and your Lord does not wrong anyone
18|50|And [remember] when We said to the angels, “Prostrate before Adam,” so they all prostrated except Iblīs, who was one of the jinn, but he disobeyed the command of his Lord. Will you then take him and his progeny as protectors instead of Me, even though they are your enemies? What a terrible exchange for the wrongdoers
18|51|I did not call them to witness the creation of the heavens and earth, nor even the creation of their own selves, and I would not take those who misguide others as helpers
18|52|And [beware of] the Day when He will say, “Call upon those whom you claimed to be My partners.” So they will call them, but they will not respond to them, and We will make them share the same doom
18|53|The wicked will see the Fire and realize that they are bound to fall into it, and they will find no escape from it
18|54|We have surely diversified in this Qur’an every kind of example for people, but man is the most quarrelsome of all beings
18|55|Nothing prevents people from believing when guidance comes to them and from seeking forgiveness from their Lord except that the fate of the earlier nations should come to them, or that the punishment should come before their eyes
18|56|We do not send the messengers except as bearers of glad tidings and warners. But those who disbelieve seek to undermine the truth with false arguments, and they take My verses and warnings in ridicule
18|57|Who could be more wrong than one who is reminded of the verses of his Lord, but he turns away from them and forgets what his hands have sent forth? We have placed veils on their hearts so that they cannot understand it, and deafness in their ears. Even if you call them to guidance, they will never be guided
18|58|But your Lord is the All-Forgiving, Lord of Mercy. If He were to take them to task for what they did, He would have hastened their punishment. Yet there is an appointed time for them from which they will find no escape
18|59|Those are the towns We destroyed when they persisted in wrongdoing, and We set an appointed time for their destruction
18|60|And [remember] when Moses said to his servant, “I will not give up until I reach the junction of the two seas, or I travel for ages.”
18|61|But when they reached the junction of the two seas, they forgot their fish, which made its way into the sea, slipping away
18|62|When they traveled further, he said to his servant, “Bring us our morning meal; this journey has truly exhausted us.”
18|63|He said, “You remember when we rested by the rock, I forgot the fish; it was none who made me forget to mention it except Satan, and it made its way into the sea amazingly.”
18|64|Moses said, “That is exactly what we were looking for.” So they turned back, retracing their footsteps
18|65|There they found one of Our slaves upon whom We bestowed Our mercy and We taught him from Our Own knowledge
18|66|Moses said to him, “May I follow you so that you may teach me some knowledge that you have been taught?”
18|67|He said, “You will never be able to have patience with me.”
18|68|How can you have patience with that which you have no knowledge about?”
18|69|Moses said, “You will find me patient, if Allah wills; and I will not disobey any of your orders.”
18|70|He said, “Then if you follow me, do not ask me about anything until I mention it to you.”
18|71|So they both set out, until when they boarded a ship, he made a hole in it. Moses said, “Did you make a hole in it to drown its people? You have done something terrible!”
18|72|He said, “Did I not tell you that you will never be able to have patience with me?”
18|73|Moses said, “Do not take me to task for what I forgot, and do not make it too difficult for me to follow you.”
18|74|Then they proceeded until they met a boy, and the man killed him. Moses said, “Did you kill an innocent soul who killed none? You have done something monstrous!”
18|75|The man said, “Did I not tell you that you will never be able to have patience with me?”
18|76|Moses said, “If I ask you about anything after this, do not keep me in your company, for then you would be excused concerning me.”
18|77|Then they went on until they came to the people of a town. They asked its people for food, but they refused to offer them hospitality. They found there a wall that was about to collapse, but he repaired it. Moses said, “If you wished, you could have taken some payment for it.”
18|78|The man said, “This is the parting of ways between me and you. I will inform you of the interpretation of that which you could not bear with patience
18|79|“As for the ship, it belonged to some poor people who worked at the sea. I wanted to make it defective because there was a king ahead of them who seized every [good] ship by force
18|80|“As for the boy, his parents were believers, and we feared that he would overburden them with his rebellion and disbelief
18|81|So we hoped that their Lord would give them another in his place, more righteous and tender-hearted
18|82|As for the wall, it belonged to two orphan boys in the city, and there was a treasure under it that belonged to them. Their father was a righteous man, so your Lord willed that they should reach their maturity and retrieve their treasure, as a mercy from your Lord; I did not do it of my own accord. This is the interpretation of that which you could not bear with patience.”
18|83|They ask you about Dhul-Qarnayn. Say, “I will tell you something about him.”
18|84|We established him on earth and gave him the means to achieve everything
18|85|He pursued a course
18|86|until when he reached the far west, he found the sun setting into a dark water, and he found some people nearby. We said, “O Dhul-Qarnayn, either punish them or treat them with kindness.”
18|87|He said, “As for one who does wrong, we will punish him, then he will be brought back to his Lord, and He will punish him grievously
18|88|But he who believes and does righteous deeds, he will have the best reward, and we will enjoin upon him to do what is easy.”
18|89|Then he pursued another course
18|90|until when he reached the far east, he found the sun rising on a people for whom We provided no shelter from it
18|91|So it was, and We had full knowledge about him
18|92|Then he pursued another course
18|93|until when he reached [a valley] between the two mountains, he found beyond them a people who could barely understand a word
18|94|They said, “O Dhul-Qarnayn, Gog and Magog are spreading corruption in the land. Can we give you some payment in return for you to construct a barrier between us and them?”
18|95|He said, “What my Lord has given me is better. But help me with manpower, I will construct a barricade between you and them
18|96|Bring me iron blocks” – until when he leveled between the two mountain-sides, he said, “Blow [with bellows],” until when he fired them up to extreme heat, he said, “Bring me molten copper to pour over it.”
18|97|Thus they could not climb over it nor could they pierce it
18|98|He said, “This is a mercy from my Lord. But when the promise of my Lord comes to pass, He will raze it to the ground. The promise of my Lord is ever true.”
18|99|On that Day We will let some of them surge like waves over others, and the Trumpet will be blown, then We will gather them all together
18|100|On that Day We will show Hell to the disbelievers clearly
18|101|those whose eyes were blind to My signs and they were unable to hear [the truth]
18|102|Do the disbelievers think that they can take My slaves as allies instead of Me? We have prepared Hell as a dwelling place for the disbelievers
18|103|Say, “Shall we inform you of the greatest losers in terms of their deeds
18|104|Those whose efforts in the life of this world are wasted, while they think that they are doing good.”
18|105|It is those who disbelieve in the verses of their Lord and their meeting with Him; their deeds will be nullified, and We will give no weight to them on the Day of Resurrection
18|106|That is their recompense: Hell, because of their disbelief and taking My verses and messengers in ridicule
18|107|As for those who believe and do righteous deeds, they will have gardens of Paradise as a dwelling place
18|108|abiding therein forever, never desiring to leave
18|109|Say, “If the ocean were ink for [writing] the Words of my Lord, the ocean would surely run dry before the Words of my Lord are finished, even if We brought its like to resupply it.”
18|110|Say, “I am only a man like you; it has been revealed to me that your God is One God. So whoever hopes for the meeting with his Lord, let him do righteous deeds and associate none in the worship of his Lord.”
19|1|Kāf Ha Ya ‘Ayn Sād
19|2|This is a reminder of the mercy of your Lord to His slave Zachariah
19|3|When he called upon his Lord in private
19|4|He said, “My Lord, my bones have grown feeble, and gray hair has spread across my head, yet never have I been disappointed in my prayer to You, my Lord
19|5|And I fear my kinsmen after me, and my wife is barren; so grant me from Yourself an heir
19|6|who will inherit [prophethood] from me and from the house of Jacob, and make him, O Lord, well pleasing to You.”
19|7|[Allah said], “O Zachariah, We give you the glad tidings of a son, whose name will be John – a name that We have not given to anyone before.”
19|8|He said, “My Lord, how can I have a son when my wife is barren, and I have reached an extremely old age?”
19|9|[The angel] said, “Thus it will be; your Lord says, ‘It is easy for Me; I did create you before, when you were nothing.’”
19|10|Zachariah said, “My Lord, give me a sign.” He said, “Your sign is that you will not be able to speak to people for three nights, despite being sound.”
19|11|Thereupon he came out to his people from the sanctuary, and signaled to them to glorify Allah morning and evening
19|12|[Allah said], “O John, hold the Scripture with all your strength.” And We gave him wisdom when he was still a child
19|13|as We made him compassionate and righteous, and he was fearing Allah
19|14|and dutiful to his parents, and he was not an oppressor or disobedient
19|15|Peace be on him the day he was born, the day he will die, and the day he will be raised up to life again
19|16|And mention in the Book [the story of] Mary when she withdrew from her family to a place towards the east
19|17|She screened herself from them, then We sent to her Our Spirit [Gabriel] and he appeared before her in the form of a perfect human being
19|18|She said, “I seek refuge in the Most Compassionate from you; [do not approach me] if you fear Allah.”
19|19|He said, “I am only a messenger from your Lord to grant you a righteous son.”
19|20|She said, “How can I have a son when no man has touched me, nor have I ever been unchaste?”
19|21|He said, “Thus it will be; your Lord says, ‘It is easy for Me; We make him a sign for people and a mercy from Us. This matter has already been decreed.’”
19|22|So she conceived him and withdrew with him to a distant place
19|23|The pains of labor drove her to the trunk of a palm tree. She said, “Oh, would that I had died before this and had been completely forgotten!”
19|24|Then the baby called her from beneath her, “Do not grieve; your Lord has provided a stream beneath you
19|25|Shake the trunk of the palm tree towards yourself; fresh ripe dates will drop upon you
19|26|Eat and drink, and be glad. And if you see any human being, say, ‘I have vowed silence to the Most Compassionate, so I will not talk to any human being today.’”
19|27|Then she came to her people carrying him. They said, “O Mary, you have committed something monstrous
19|28|O sister of Aaron, your father was not a man of evil, nor was your mother unchaste.”
19|29|Thereupon she pointed to him. They said, “How can we talk to someone who is still a baby in the cradle?”
19|30|Jesus said, “I am a slave of Allah. He has given me the Scripture and made me a prophet
19|31|He has made me blessed wherever I may be, and has enjoined upon me prayer and zakah as long as I am alive
19|32|and has made me dutiful to my mother, and has not made me an oppressor or disobedient
19|33|Peace is upon me the day I was born, the day I will die and the day I will be resurrected.”
19|34|Such was Jesus, son of Mary – a word of truth about which they are in doubt
19|35|It is not befitting Allah to beget a son. Glory be to Him! When He decrees a matter, He only says to it, “Be,” and it is
19|36|[Jesus said], “Indeed, Allah is my Lord and your Lord, so worship Him. This is a straight path.”
19|37|But the factions differed among themselves [about him]. So woe to the disbelievers from the scene of a momentous Day
19|38|How sharp they will hear and see on the Day they come to Us! But today the wrongdoers are clearly misguided
19|39|Warn them of the Day of Remorse when all matters will be decided, but they are heedless and they do not believe
19|40|It is We Who will inherit the earth and all those who are on it, and to Us they will be returned
19|41|And mention in the Book [the story of] Abraham. He was indeed a man of truth and a prophet
19|42|When he said to his father, “O my dear father, why do you worship something that neither hears nor sees, nor benefits you in any way
19|43|O my dear father, there has come to me some knowledge that has not come to you, so follow me; I will guide you to a straight path
19|44|O my dear father, do not worship Satan. Indeed, Satan is rebellious against the Most Compassionate
19|45|O my dear father, I truly fear that a punishment from the Most Compassionate may afflict you and that you may become a companion of Satan [in Hell].”
19|46|He said, “Are you turning away from my gods, O Abraham? If you do not desist, I will surely stone you. Keep away from me for a long time!”
19|47|Abraham said, “Peace be on you. I will seek my Lord’s forgiveness for you. Indeed, He is Most Gracious to me
19|48|I will distance myself from you and from all that you supplicate besides Allah, and I will supplicate my Lord; perhaps my supplication to my Lord will not go unanswered.”
19|49|When he distanced himself from them and what they worshiped besides Allah, We granted him Isaac and Jacob, and made each one of them a prophet
19|50|We bestowed upon them of Our mercy, and blessed them with a highly esteemed reputation
19|51|And mention in the Book [the story of] Moses. He was indeed a chosen one, and was a messenger and a prophet
19|52|We called him from the right side of the Mount Tūr [in Sinai] and We brought him near by conversing with him in private
19|53|And We granted him, by Our mercy, his brother Aaron, as a prophet
19|54|And mention in the Book [the story of] Ishmael. He was true to his promise, and was a messenger and a prophet
19|55|He used to command his people to pray and give zakah, and his Lord was well pleased with him
19|56|And mention in the Book [the story of] Idrīs. He was a man of truth and a prophet
19|57|And We raised him to a high status
19|58|These are the prophets whom Allah has favored from among the descendants of Adam, and from those whom We carried with Noah [in the Ark], and from the descendants of Abraham and Israel [Jacob], and from those whom We guided and chose. Whenever the verses of the Most Compassionate were recited to them, they fell down in prostration, weeping
19|59|But they were succeeded by generations who neglected prayer and pursued their desires; so they will meet their doom
19|60|except those who repent and believe, and do righteous deeds – it is they who will enter Paradise and they will not be wronged in the least
19|61|Gardens of Eternity which the Most Compassionate has promised His slaves who have not seen them. His promise will surely be fulfilled
19|62|They will not hear therein any idle talk, except greetings of peace, and they will have their provision morning and evening
19|63|Such is the Paradise which We will give as an inheritance to those of Our slaves who feared Allah
19|64|[Gabriel said], “We do not descend except with the command of your Lord. To Him belongs all that is before us and all that is behind us, and all that is in between. Your Lord is never forgetful
19|65|Lord of the heavens and earth and all that is between them. So worship Him and be constant in worshiping Him. Do you know anyone equal to Him?”
19|66|Man says, “Once I am dead, will I be raised to life again?”
19|67|Does man not remember that We created him beforehand, when he was nothing
19|68|By your Lord, We will surely gather them and the devils, then We will surely bring them all around Hell on their knees
19|69|Then We will surely drag out of every group those who were most rebellious against the Most Compassionate
19|70|For indeed We know best those who are most deserving to burn therein
19|71|There is none among you except that he will pass over it; a decree from your Lord that must be fulfilled
19|72|Then We will save those who fear Allah and will leave the wrongdoers in it on their knees
19|73|When Our verses are recited to them in all their clarity, the disbelievers say to the believers, “Which of the two parties is better in terms of dwellings and superior in social gatherings?”
19|74|How many generations We have destroyed before them who were superior in terms of wealth and outward appearance
19|75|Say, “Whoever is following misguidance, the Most Compassionate will give him respite, until they see what they were warned of – be it the punishment [in this world] or the Hour – only then will they realize who is in a worse abode and who has a smaller following.”
19|76|Allah increases in guidance those who are guided, and the righteous deeds of lasting merit are better with your Lord in reward and better in return
19|77|Have you seen the one who rejects Our verses and says, “I will surely be given wealth and children [if I am resurrected]?”
19|78|Has he obtained knowledge of the unseen, or has he taken a pledge with the Most Compassionate
19|79|Never! We will write down what he says and will prolong his punishment extensively
19|80|We will inherit what he boasts of, and he will come to Us all alone
19|81|They have taken gods other than Allah, in order that they may protect them [from punishment]
19|82|Never! They will deny their worship and will become their enemies
19|83|Do you not see that We sent devils against the disbelievers constantly inciting them to sin
19|84|So do not be in haste about them; We are surely counting down their days
19|85|The Day when We will gather the righteous before the Most Compassionate as honored guests
19|86|and We will drive the wicked to Hell like a thirsty herd
19|87|None will have the power to intercede except those who have taken permission from the Most Compassionate
19|88|They say, “The Most Compassionate has begotten a son.”
19|89|You have made a monstrous statement
19|90|at which the heavens are about to be torn apart, the earth split asunder, and the mountains tumble down
19|91|because they have ascribed to the Most Compassionate a son
19|92|It is not appropriate for the Most Compassionate to beget a son
19|93|There is none in the heavens and earth except that he will come to the Most Compassionate in full submission
19|94|He has counted them and numbered them precisely
19|95|Each one of them will come to Him on the Day of Resurrection all alone
19|96|Those who believe and do righteous deeds, the Most Compassionate will endear them [to His creation]
19|97|We have made this [Qur’an] easy on your language so that you may give thereby glad tidings to the righteous and warn people who are contentious
19|98|How many generations We destroyed before them! Do you sense a single one of them or even hear from them a whisper
20|1|Tā Ha
20|2|We have not sent down the Qur’an to you [O Prophet] to cause you distress
20|3|but as a reminder for those who fear Allah
20|4|A revelation from the One Who created the earth and the high heavens
20|5|The Most Compassionate rose over the Throne
20|6|To Him belongs all that is in the heavens and all that is on earth, and all that is between them, and all that is beneath the soil
20|7|Whether you speak loudly [or not], He surely knows what is secret and what is even more hidden
20|8|Allah – none has the right to be worshiped except Him. He has the Most Beautiful Names
20|9|Has there come to you the story of Moses
20|10|When he saw a fire, he said to his family, “Stay here. I have spotted a fire; I may bring you a flaming brand from it, or find some guidance at the fire.”
20|11|When he came to it, he was called, “O Moses
20|12|Indeed, I am your Lord, so take off your shoes; you are in the sacred valley of Tuwā
20|13|I have chosen you, so listen to what is being revealed
20|14|‘Indeed, I am Allah; none has the right to be worshiped except Me, so worship Me and establish prayer to remember me
20|15|The Hour is certainly coming, but I almost keep it hidden, so that every soul will be recompensed for what it strives
20|16|So do not let those who disbelieve in it and follow their desires distract you from it, or you will perish.’”
20|17|What is that in your right hand, O Moses?”
20|18|He said, “It is my staff. I lean on it and beat down leaves with it for my sheep, and I have other uses for it.”
20|19|Allah said, “Throw it down, O Moses!”
20|20|He threw it down, and it suddenly became a slithering snake
20|21|Allah said, “Pick it up, and have no fear. We will restore it to its former state
20|22|Put your hand under your armpit; it will come out shining white without blemish, as another sign
20|23|so that We may show you some of Our greatest signs
20|24|Go to Pharaoh, for he has transgressed all bounds.”
20|25|He said, “My Lord, reassure my heart for me
20|26|and ease my task for me
20|27|and loosen the knot from my tongue
20|28|so that they may understand my speech
20|29|And appoint for me a helper from my family
20|30|Aaron, my brother
20|31|Increase my strength through him
20|32|and let him share my task
20|33|so that we may glorify You much
20|34|and remember You much
20|35|For indeed You are All-Watchful over us.”
20|36|Allah said, “You are granted your request, O Moses
20|37|And We had already conferred favor upon you before
20|38|when We inspired your mother, saying
20|39|‘Put him into the casket, then cast it into the river. The river will carry it to the shore, and he will be picked up by one who is an enemy to Me and enemy to him.’ I bestowed upon you love from Myself so that you would be brought up under My [watchful] Eye
20|40|When your sister was going along and said, ‘Shall I show you someone who will nurse him?’ Thus We brought you back to your mother, so that she may rejoice and not grieve. Then you killed a man [by mistake], but We saved you from distress, and We put you through several trials. You stayed among the people of Midian for several years, then you came [here] at a destined time, O Moses
20|41|I have chosen you for Myself
20|42|Go forth, you and your brother, with My signs and do not slacken in remembering Me
20|43|Go, both of you, to Pharaoh, for he has certainly transgressed all bounds
20|44|But speak to him gently, so that he may take heed or fear Allah.”
20|45|They said, “Our Lord, we fear that he may hasten to punish us or transgress all bounds.”
20|46|He said, “Do not be afraid; I am with you both, hearing and seeing
20|47|So go to him and say, ‘We are both messengers from your Lord, so let the Children of Israel go with us and do not oppress them. We have come to you with a sign from your Lord; and peace be upon he who follows the true guidance
20|48|It has been revealed to us that the punishment awaits those who reject [the truth] and turn away.’”
20|49|Pharaoh said, “So who is the Lord of you two, O Moses?”
20|50|He said, “Our Lord is the One Who gave everything its form then guided it.”
20|51|Pharaoh said, “Then what about the former [disbelieving] nations?”
20|52|He said, “Its knowledge is with my Lord in a Record. My Lord never errs, nor does He forget.”
20|53|It is He Who spread out the earth for you and made therein pathways for you, and sent down rain from the sky; and We brought forth thereby various types of plants
20|54|Eat and graze your livestock. Indeed, there are signs in this for people of sound intellect
20|55|From this [earth] We created you, and to it We will return you, and from it We will raise you once again
20|56|We showed Pharaoh all Our signs, but he rejected them and refused to believe
20|57|He said, “Have you come to drive us out of our land with your magic, O Moses
20|58|We will surely bring you similar magic. So appoint a day between us that neither you nor we will fail to keep, in a convenient place.”
20|59|Moses said, “Your appointment is the festival day; let the people be gathered at forenoon.”
20|60|So Pharaoh went away and put together his scheme, then came forth
20|61|Moses said to them, “Woe to you, do not fabricate lies against Allah, lest He exterminate you with a punishment. Those who fabricate lies are bound to fail.”
20|62|Then they disputed the matter among themselves, and kept their talk private
20|63|They said, “These two are merely magicians who want to drive you out of your land with their magic and destroy your exemplary way of life
20|64|So gather your scheme, then line up in a row. Whoever prevails today is indeed the victor.”
20|65|They said, “O Moses, either you throw or shall we be the first to throw!”
20|66|He said, “No; you throw first.” Suddenly their ropes and staffs appeared to him, owing to their magic, as if they were slithering
20|67|Then Moses sensed fear within himself
20|68|We said, “Do not be afraid; it is you who will prevail
20|69|Throw what is in your right hand; it will swallow up what they have contrived. They have only contrived a magic trick, and the magician will never prosper, wherever he goes.”
20|70|So the magicians fell down in prostration, saying, “We believe in the Lord of Aaron and Moses.”
20|71|Pharaoh said, “How dare you believe in him before I give you permission! He must be your master who taught you magic! I will surely cut off your hands and feet on opposite sides, and I will crucify you on the trunks of palm trees; you will surely know whose punishment is more severe and more lasting!”
20|72|They said, “We will never choose you over the clear signs that have come to us, or over the One Who created us. So decide whatever you will. You can only make a decision about the life of this world
20|73|We surely believe in our Lord so that He may forgive us our sins and the magic that you have compelled us to practice, for Allah is best [in reward] and more lasting [in punishment].”
20|74|Whoever comes to his Lord as an evildoer, for him is Hell; he will neither die therein nor live
20|75|But whoever comes to Him as a believer, having done righteous deeds, it is they who will have the highest ranks
20|76|Gardens of Eternity, under which rivers flow, abiding therein forever. Such is the reward of those who purify themselves
20|77|We inspired Moses, “Travel by night with My slaves, and strike for them a dry path across the sea. Have no fear of being overtaken, nor be afraid [of drowning].”
20|78|Then Pharaoh pursued them with his soldiers, but they were completely overwhelmed by the sea
20|79|Thus Pharaoh led his people astray, and did not guide them
20|80|O Children of Israel, We rescued you from your enemy, and made an appointment with you on the right side of Mount Tūr [in Sinai], and sent down for you manna and quails
20|81|[saying], “Eat from the good things We have provided for you, but do not exceed the limits therein, or My wrath will befall you, for anyone upon whom My wrath befalls is perished
20|82|I am indeed Most Forgiving to those who repent and believe, and do righteous deeds, then stay on the right path.”
20|83|[Allah asked], “What made you hasten from your people, O Moses?”
20|84|He said, “They are following my footsteps; I hastened to You, my Lord, to please You.”
20|85|Allah said, “We have certainly tested your people in your absence, and Sāmiri has led them astray.”
20|86|So Moses returned to his people, angry and sorrowful. He said, “O my people, did your Lord not promise you a good promise? Was my absence too long for you, or did you want the wrath from your Lord to befall you, so you broke your promise to me?”
20|87|They said, “We did not break our promise to you out of our own free will, but we were made to carry loads of the people’s jewelry, so we threw them [into the fire], and so did the Sāmiri throw.”
20|88|Then he moulded for them an image of a calf that made a lowing sound. They said, “This is your god and Moses’ god, but he has forgotten.”
20|89|Do they not see that it does not respond a word to them, nor does it have power to harm or benefit them
20|90|Aaron told them beforehand, “O my people, you are being tested with it. Your Lord is the Most Compassionate, so follow me and obey my command.”
20|91|They said, “We will never cease to worship it until Moses comes back to us.”
20|92|Moses said, “O Aaron, what prevented you when you saw them going astray
20|93|from following me? Did you disobey my command?”
20|94|Aaron said, “O son of my mother, do not seize me by my beard or by my head! I feared that you would say, ‘You have caused division among the Children of Israel, and did not heed my words.’”
20|95|Moses said, “What is the matter with you, O Sāmiri?”
20|96|He said, “I saw something they did not see, so I took a handful [of dust] from the hoof-print of the horse of the messenger [Gabriel] and cast it [into the fire]. This is what my mind prompted me.”
20|97|Moses said, “Begone then! Your [punishment] in this life will be to say, ‘Do not touch me,’ but there awaits you an appointed time for your reckoning that you cannot escape. Now look at your so-called god which you kept worshiping; We will surely burn it then scatter it in the sea
20|98|[O people], your god is only Allah; none has the right to be worshiped except Him. He encompasses everything in knowledge.”
20|99|This is how We relate to you [O Prophet] from the stories of the past, and We have given you a Reminder from Us
20|100|Whoever turns away from it will bear a heavy burden on the Day of Resurrection
20|101|abiding therein forever. What a terrible burden they will carry on the Day of Resurrection
20|102|the Day when the Trumpet will be blown; on that Day We will gather together the wicked sightless [from horror]
20|103|They will whisper with one another, “You stayed no more than ten days [on earth].”
20|104|We know best what they will say – the most discerning among them will say, “You stayed no more than a day.”
20|105|They ask you about the mountains, say, “My Lord will scatter them into dust
20|106|and He will leave the earth level and plain
20|107|you will not see therein any troughs or peaks.”
20|108|On that day, they will follow the summoner; none will dare to deviate. All voices will be hushed in awe before the Most Compassionate; you will hear nothing except a whisper
20|109|On that day, no intercession will be of any use except to whom the Most Compassionate gave permission and approved his word
20|110|He knows all that is ahead of them and all that is behind them, but they do not encompass it with their knowledge
20|111|All faces will be humbled before the Ever-Living, Self-Sustaining. Those burdened with evil deeds will be in total loss
20|112|But whoever does righteous deeds, being a believer, will have no fear of being wronged or deprived
20|113|We have sent it down as an Arabic Qur’an and diversified its warnings, so that they may fear Allah or it may cause them to take heed
20|114|So Exalted is Allah, the True Sovereign. Do not hasten to [recite] the Qur’an before its revelation to you is concluded, and say, “My Lord, increase me in knowledge.”
20|115|We had already given a command to Adam before, but he forgot, and We found him lacking a firm resolve
20|116|When We said to the angels, “Prostrate before Adam,” so they all prostrated, except Iblīs, who refused
20|117|We said “O Adam, this is an enemy to you and to your wife, so do not let him drive you both out of Paradise, for then you will fall into misery
20|118|Here you will neither go hungry nor naked
20|119|nor will you suffer from thirst or from scorching heat.”
20|120|Then Satan whispered to him, and said, “O Adam, shall I show you the tree of immortality and a kingdom that will never decay?”
20|121|So they both ate from the tree, then their nakedness was revealed to each other, and they began to put together leaves from Paradise to cover themselves. Thus Adam disobeyed his Lord, and fell into error
20|122|Thereafter his Lord chose him, accepted his repentance, and guided him
20|123|Allah said, “Get down, both of you, from here altogether [with Satan] as enemies to one another. Then when there comes to you guidance from Me, whoever follows My guidance will neither go astray nor fall into misery
20|124|But whoever turns away from My Reminder will have a miserable life, and on the Day of Resurrection We will raise him blind.”
20|125|He will say, “My Lord, why have you raised me blind, when I was able to see before?”
20|126|Allah will say, “Similarly Our verses came to you, but you ignored them, so you will be ignored Today.”
20|127|This is how We recompense those who transgress the limits and do not believe in the verses of his Lord; and the punishment of the Hereafter is more severe and more lasting
20|128|Is it not yet clear to them how many generations We destroyed before them, in whose dwellings they still walk about? There are signs in this for people of sound intellect
20|129|Were it not for a prior decree from your Lord [O Prophet] and a time already set, they would have already been punishment
20|130|So be patient with what they say, and glorify your Lord with praise before sunrise and before sunset, and glorify Him during the night and at both ends of the day, so that you may be pleased [with the reward]
20|131|Do not turn your eyes covetously towards the various forms of splendor of this life that We have given some of the [disbelievers] to enjoy, as a trial for them. But the provision of your Lord is far better and more lasting
20|132|Enjoin your household to perform prayer and adhere to it firmly. We ask no provision from you; rather, it is We Who give you provision. And the best outcome is for those who fear Allah
20|133|They say, “Why does he not bring us a sign from his Lord?” Has there not come to them [the Qur’an as] a confirmation of what is in the earlier Scriptures
20|134|If We had destroyed them with a punishment before this, they would have said, “Our Lord, if only You had sent us a messenger so that we would have followed Your verses before being humiliated and disgraced.”
20|135|Say, “Each of us is waiting, so wait! You will come to know who are the people of the straight path and who are rightly guided.”
21|1|The reckoning of the people has drawn near, yet they are turning away heedlessly
21|2|Whenever new revelation comes to them from their Lord, they listen to it in jest
21|3|with their hearts heedless. The wrongdoers whisper to one another in secret, “Is this but a human being just like yourselves? Will you then follow his magic, although you openly see?”
21|4|He said, “My Lord knows every word spoken in the heavens and earth, for He is the All-Hearing, the All-Knowing.”
21|5|Yet they say, “This [Qur’an] is a set of jumbled dreams! Rather, he has fabricated it! Rather, he is a poet! So let him bring us a sign such as the earlier messengers were sent with.”
21|6|Not a single town We destroyed before them believed [after receiving signs]; will they then believe
21|7|We did not send before you [O Prophet] except men to whom We gave revelation, so [O people] ask the People of the Scriptures if you do not know
21|8|We did not give them bodies that needed no food, nor were they immortal
21|9|Then We fulfilled Our promise to them: We saved them and those whom We willed, and destroyed those who transgressed all bounds
21|10|We have sent down to you [O people] a Book in which there is honor for you. Do you not then understand
21|11|[Imagine] how many towns of evildoers We have destroyed, and raised up after them another people
21|12|When they sensed Our punishment, they started running away from it
21|13|“Do not run away, but return to your luxuries and dwellings, perhaps you will be questioned.”
21|14|They said, “Woe to us! We were indeed wrongdoers.”
21|15|They kept crying out loud this until We mowed them down, lifeless
21|16|We did not create the heavens and earth and all that is between them for fun
21|17|If We had wished for a pastime, We could have had it from Our own, if We were to do so
21|18|Rather, We hurl the truth at falsehood, and it crushes it, so it vanishes. Woe to you for what you falsely ascribe [to Allah]
21|19|To Him belongs all those who are in the heavens and earth. Those [angels] who are with Him are not too proud to worship Him, nor do they ever grow weary
21|20|They glorify Him day and night tirelessly
21|21|Or have they taken gods from the earth who [cannot even] resurrect the dead
21|22|If there had been gods besides Allah in the heavens and earth, both realms would have fallen in disorder. Glory be to Allah – Lord of the Throne – far above what they ascribe [to Him]
21|23|He cannot be questioned for what He does, but they will be questioned
21|24|Or have they taken other gods besides Him? Say, “Bring your proof. Here is the Book of those who are with me, and the Book of those who came before me.” Yet most of them do not know the truth, so they turn away
21|25|“We never sent before you [O Prophet] any messenger without revealing to him that none has the right to be worshiped except Me, so worship Me.”
21|26|They say, “The Most Compassionate has begotten offspring!” Glory be to Him! In fact, those [angels] are His honored slaves
21|27|They do not speak before He speaks, and they only do as He commands
21|28|He knows what is ahead of them and what is behind them. They cannot intercede except for whom He pleases, and they are fearful in awe of Him
21|29|If anyone of them were to say, “I am god besides Him,” We would punish him with Hell. This is how We punish the wrongdoers
21|30|Are the disbelievers not aware that the heavens and earth were joined together and then We split them apart? We created from water every living thing. Will they not then believe
21|31|We have set on the earth firm mountains so it does not shake with them, and We have made therein broad pathways so that they may find their way
21|32|And We have made the sky a well-protected canopy, yet they turn away from its signs
21|33|It is He Who created the night and the day, the sun and the moon – each floating in its orbit
21|34|We did not grant immortality to any human being before you [O Prophet]. So if you die, will they live forever
21|35|Every soul will taste death; We test you with bad and good as a trial, then to Us you will all be returned
21|36|When the disbelievers see you, they only take you in ridicule, [saying], “Is this the one who speaks ill of your gods?” while they reject even the mention of the Most Compassionate
21|37|Man is created of haste. I will show you My signs, so do not ask Me to hasten them
21|38|They say, “When will this promise come to pass, if you are truthful?”
21|39|If only the disbelievers knew the moment when they will be unable to ward the Fire off their faces or their backs, nor will they be helped
21|40|Rather, it will come upon them suddenly and stun them; they will not be able to avert it, nor will they be given respite
21|41|Indeed, there were messengers before you who were ridiculed, but those who mocked them were encompassed by what they used to ridicule
21|42|Say, “Who can protect you by night and by day against the Most Compassionate?” Yet they turn away from the admonition of their Lord
21|43|Do they have gods who can defend them against Us? They cannot even help themselves, nor will they be protected from Us
21|44|Nevertheless, We have provided for them and their forefathers luxuries which they enjoyed for a long time. Do they not see that We gradually reduce the land from its outlying sides? Is it they who will then prevail
21|45|Say, “I only warn you by divine revelation.” But the deaf cannot hear the call when they are warned
21|46|If a mere breath of your Lord’s torment were to touch them, they would surely say, “Woe to us! We were indeed wrongdoers.”
21|47|We will place the scales of justice on the Day of Resurrection, and no soul will be wronged in the least. Even if a deed is the weight of a mustard seed, We will bring it forth. Sufficient are We as Reckoners
21|48|We certainly gave Moses and Aaron the Criterion, a shining light and admonition for the righteous
21|49|those who fear their Lord without seeing Him, and are apprehensive of the Hour
21|50|And this [Qur’an] is a blessed reminder which We have sent down. Are you still denying it
21|51|Indeed, We had given Abraham sound judgment before, for We know him well
21|52|When he said to his father and his people, “What are these statues to which you are so devoted?”
21|53|They said, “We found our forefathers worshiping them.”
21|54|He said, “Indeed, you and your forefathers were clearly misguided.”
21|55|They said, “Have you come to us with the truth, or are you joking?”
21|56|He said, “Nay, your Lord is the Lord of the heavens and earth, Who created them, and I am one of those who bear witness to it
21|57|By Allah, I will surely plot against your idols after you have turned and gone away.”
21|58|So he broke them into pieces, except the biggest of them, so that they might come back to it
21|59|They said, “Who has done this to our gods? He is indeed one of the wrongdoers.”
21|60|They said, “We heard a young man, speaking ill of them, who is called Abraham.”
21|61|They said, “Bring him then before the eyes of the people, so that they may witness [his trial].”
21|62|They said, “Are you the one who did this to our gods, O Abraham?”
21|63|He said, “Rather, it was this biggest one who did it. So ask them, if they can speak!”
21|64|So they turned back to one another, and said, “Indeed, it is you who are the wrongdoers.”
21|65|Then they turned to their obstinacy, [saying], “You already know that they cannot speak.”
21|66|Abraham said, “Do you then worship besides Allah that which can neither benefit nor harm you in the least
21|67|Fie upon you and upon all that you worship besides Allah! Do you not have any sense?”
21|68|They said, “Burn him and avenge your gods, if you must do something.”
21|69|We said, “O fire, be cool and safe for Abraham.”
21|70|They plotted to harm him, but We made them the worst losers
21|71|And We saved him and Lot [and brought him] to the land [of Levant] that we have blessed for all people
21|72|And We gave him Isaac, and then Jacob, a grandson, and We made all of them righteous
21|73|And We made them leaders, guiding people by Our command, and We inspired them to do righteous deeds, establish prayer and give zakah; and they were Our true worshipers
21|74|To Lot We gave sound judgment and knowledge, and We saved him from the town that was engrossed in shameful practices. They were Indeed an evil and rebellious people
21|75|And We admitted him to Our mercy, for he was one of the righteous
21|76|And [remember] Noah, when he called out to Us before, so We responded to him and saved him and his household from the great distress
21|77|And We helped him against the people who rejected Our signs. They were indeed an evil people, so We drowned them all
21|78|And [remember] David and Solomon, when they passed judgment about the tillage into which some people’s sheep had strayed at night, and We were witnesses to their judgment
21|79|We made Solomon understand it, although We gave each of them sound judgment and knowledge. We subjected the mountains and birds to glorify Allah along with David. It was We Who did all this
21|80|And We taught him the art of making coats of mail for you to protect yourselves in your battle. Will you then be grateful
21|81|And to Solomon [We subjected] the raging wind, to blow by his command to the land We had blessed. It is We Who have full knowledge of everything
21|82|And among the devils [We subjected] those who dived for him and performed other duties. It is We Who were watching over them
21|83|And [remember] Job, when he cried out to his Lord, “I have been struck by adversity, and You are the Most Merciful of those who show mercy.”
21|84|So We responded to him and relieved his adversity, and We restored to him his family, twice as many, as a mercy from Us and as a reminder for Our worshipers
21|85|And [remember] Ishmael, Idrīs and Dhul-Kifl; they were all steadfast
21|86|And We admitted them to Our mercy, for they were truly righteous
21|87|And [remember] the Man of the Whale [Jonah] when he departed in anger, thinking that We would not take him to task. Then he cried out in the depths of darkness, “None has the right to be worshiped except You. Glory be to You! I have certainly done wrong”
21|88|So We answered his prayer and rescued him from distress. This is how We rescue the believers
21|89|And [remember] Zachariah, when he cried out to his Lord, “My Lord, do not leave me childless, for You are the Best of Inheritors.”
21|90|So We answered his prayer and gave him John, and made his wife fertile. They used to hasten in doing good deeds and used to call upon Us with hope and fear, and they were humble before Us
21|91|And [remember Mary] who guarded her chastity; We breathed in her through Our spirit [Gabriel], and made her and her son a sign for all people
21|92|Indeed, this religion of yours is one religion, and I am your Lord, so worship Me alone
21|93|But people have divided themselves into sects; yet they will all return to Us
21|94|Whoever does righteous deeds while he is a believer, his efforts will not be denied, for We are recording them all
21|95|It is not possible for any town that We have destroyed to ever come back [to this world]
21|96|until when Gog and Magog are let loose, swarming swiftly from every mound
21|97|when the True Promise draws near, the eyes of those who disbelieved will stare in horror, [saying], “Woe to us! We were indeed heedless of this; nay, we were wrongdoers.”
21|98|Indeed, you and all that you worship besides Allah will be the fuel for Hell; you will surely enter it
21|99|If these [idols] had truly been gods, they would not have entered it. But they will all abide therein forever
21|100|They will groan therein with anguish, and they will not be able to hear anything
21|101|But those for whom We have decreed the finest reward, they will be far away from it
21|102|They will not hear its slightest hissing, and they will abide forever in whatever their souls desire
21|103|They will not be grieved by the Greatest Terror, and the angels will receive them [saying], “This is your Day that you were promised”
21|104|On the Day when We roll up the heavens like a scroll of records. Just as We originated the first creation, so We will bring it back. That is Our binding promise, which We will surely do
21|105|We have written in the Psalms after the Preserved Record, that the land will be inherited by My righteous slaves
21|106|Indeed, there is a message in this [Qur’an] for devoted worshipers
21|107|We have not sent you [O Prophet] except as a mercy to the worlds
21|108|Say, “It is only revealed to me that your God is only One God; will you then submit to Him
21|109|But if they turn away, say, “I have proclaimed the message to you all alike, and I do not know whether what you are warned of is near or far
21|110|Indeed, He knows what is said openly and knows what you conceal
21|111|I do not know; perhaps this [delay] is a test for you and an enjoyment for a while.”
21|112|[The Prophet] said, “My Lord, judge [between us] in truth. Our Lord is the Most Compassionate Whose help is to be sought against what you describe.”
22|1|O mankind, fear your Lord; the earthquake of the Hour is something dreadful
22|2|On the Day when you see it, every nursing mother will abandon her baby, and every pregnant woman will miscarry. You will see people as though they are drunk, while they are not drunk, but the punishment of Allah is severe
22|3|There are some people who dispute concerning Allah without knowledge, and they follow every rebellious devil
22|4|It has been decreed that whoever takes him as an ally, he will misguide him and lead him to the punishment of the Blazing Fire
22|5|O mankind, if you are in doubt concerning the Resurrection, then We surely created you from dust, then from a drop of sperm, then from a clot, then from a lump of flesh – formed or unformed – so that We may make it clear to you [Our power]. We settle in the wombs whatever We will for an appointed term. Then We bring you out as infants, then [We nurture you] so that you may reach your maturity. Then some of you die, while others are left to reach the decrepit old age so that they may know nothing after having knowledge. You see the land lifeless, then as soon as We send down rain on it, it stirs and swells to life and brings forth every type of pleasant plant
22|6|That is because Allah is the Truth; He alone gives life to the dead, and He is Most Capable of all things
22|7|The Hour is certainly coming; there is no doubt about it, and Allah will surely resurrect those who are in the graves
22|8|There are some people who argue about Allah without knowledge, guidance or an enlightening scripture
22|9|They turn their faces away [in arrogance] to lead people away from Allah’s way. For them there will be disgrace in this world, and on the Day of Resurrection We will make them taste the punishment of the burning fire
22|10|“This is because of what your hands have sent forth, and Allah is not unjust to His slaves.”
22|11|There are some people who worship Allah on the edge [of faith]: if something good comes to them, they are content; but if they are afflicted with a trial, they turn back, thus losing both this world and the Hereafter. That is the evident loss
22|12|They invoke besides Allah what can neither harm nor benefit them. That is the farthest misguidance
22|13|They invoke those whose harm is more likely than their benefit. What a terrible protector and what a terrible associate
22|14|Allah will surely admit those who believe and do righteous deeds to gardens under which rivers flow. Allah surely does what He wills
22|15|Whoever thinks that Allah will never help His Prophet in this world and the Hereafter, let him stretch out a rope to the ceiling and strangle himself, then let him see if his effort can remove what enrages him
22|16|This is how We sent down this [Qur’an] as clear verses, and Allah guides whom He wills
22|17|Indeed, those who believe, those who are Jews, the Sabians, the Christians, the Magians and those who associate partners with Allah – Allah will judge between them on the Day of Resurrection; Allah is Witness over all things
22|18|Do you not see that to Allah prostrate all those who are in the heavens and all those on earth: the sun, the moon, the stars, the mountains, the trees, the moving creatures, and many humans? But there are many on whom the punishment has become due. Whoever Allah disgraces, none can honor him. Allah surely does what He wills
22|19|These are two opponents who are in dispute about their Lord. As for the disbelievers, garments of Fire will be tailored for them, and scalding water will be poured over their heads
22|20|melting all that is in their bellies and their skins
22|21|And for [striking] them there will be maces of iron
22|22|Every time, in their anguish, they try to get out of it, they will be forced back into it, “Taste the burning punishment!”
22|23|Allah will surely admit those who believe and do righteous deeds to gardens under which rivers flow. They will be adorned with bracelets of gold and pearls, and their garments will be of silk
22|24|They were guided to the best of words and they were guided to the praiseworthy path
22|25|As for those who disbelieve and prevent people from Allah’s way and from the Sacred Mosque – which We have made for all people, residents and visitors alike – and whoever intends to deviate therein by evildoing, We will cause him to taste a painful punishment
22|26|And [remember] when We showed to Abraham the site of the House [Ka’ba], “Do not associate anything with Me, and purify My House for those who circumambulate it, and those who stand up in prayer, and those who bow and prostrate
22|27|And proclaim the pilgrimage to all people; they will come to you on foot and on every lean camel from every distant pathway
22|28|so that they may attain benefits, and pronounce Allah’s name during the appointed days over the sacrificial animals that He has provided for them; then eat from it and feed the desperate poor
22|29|Then let them complete their rites, fulfill their vows, and circumambulate the Ancient House [Ka’ba].”
22|30|Such [is the pilgrimage]; whoever honors the sacred rituals of Allah, it is best for him with his Lord. All sacrificial animals have been made lawful for you except what is recited to you. So shun the impurity of idolatry and shun the words of falsehood
22|31|Be exclusively devoted to Allah, associating no partners with Him. Whoever associates partners with Allah, it is as if he has fallen from the sky and has been snatched away by birds or swept away by the wind to a far off place
22|32|This is so. And whoever honors the rituals of Allah, it is from the piety of the hearts
22|33|There are benefits for you in these [sacrificial animals] for an appointed term, then their place of sacrifice is near the Ancient House
22|34|For every community We ordained rites of sacrifice so that they may mention the name of Allah over the sacrificial animals that He has provided for them. Your God is One God, so submit to Him alone, and give glad tidings to the humble
22|35|those whose hearts are filled with awe when Allah is mentioned, and those who patiently endure whatever may befall them, and who establish prayer and spend out of what We have provided for them
22|36|We have ordained the sacrificial camels [and cattle] among the rituals of Allah, in which there is much good for you. So mention the name of Allah over them when they are lined up, then when they fall down on their sides, eat of them and feed those [poor] who do not beg and those who do. Thus We have made them subservient to you, so that you may be grateful
22|37|It is neither their flesh nor their blood that reaches Allah, but it is your piety that reaches Him. This is how He has subjected them to you, so that you may proclaim Allah’s greatness for having guided you. And give glad tidings to those who do good
22|38|Indeed, Allah defends those who believe, and Allah does not like every treacherous and ungrateful
22|39|Permission [to fight] is given to those who are attacked, because they were oppressed, and Allah is indeed Most Capable of granting them victory
22|40|those who have been driven out of their homes for no reason other than they say, “Our Lord is Allah.” If Allah were not to repel some people by means of others, monasteries, churches, synagogues and mosques wherein the name of Allah is often mentioned, would surely have been demolished. Allah surely helps those who stand up for His cause. Indeed, Allah is All-Powerful, All-Mighty
22|41|It is those who, if We give them power in the land, they establish prayer and give zakah, and enjoin what is right and forbid what is wrong. And to Allah belongs the outcome of all matters
22|42|If they reject you [O Prophet], the people of Noah, ‘Ād and Thamūd before them also rejected [their prophets]
22|43|as did the people of Abraham and the people of Lot
22|44|and the people of Midian. And Moses was [also] rejected. But I gave respite to the disbelievers, then I seized them. How severe was My response
22|45|How many towns We have destroyed for their persistent wrongdoing, leaving them in total ruin; their wells abandoned and their lofty palaces deserted
22|46|Have they not traveled through the land so that their hearts might understand and their ears might listen? It is not the eyes that turn blind, but it is the hearts within the breasts that turn blind
22|47|They ask you to hasten the punishment, but Allah will not fail in His promise. A single day with your Lord is like one thousand years by your count
22|48|to how many towns did I give respite when they were wrongdoers, then I seized them. And to Me is the final return
22|49|Say, “O people, I am only sent to you as a clear warner
22|50|Those who believe and do righteous deeds will have forgiveness and a generous provision
22|51|But those who strive to discredit Our verses, they are the people of the Blazing Fire.”
22|52|We did not send any messenger or prophet before you except that when he recited, Satan would cast into it. But Allah would abolish what Satan casts, then Allah would confirm His verses, for Allah is All-Knowing, All-Wise
22|53|[That is] so that He may make what Satan casts a trial for those [hypocrites] whose hearts are sick and those [disbelievers] whose hearts are hardened, for indeed the wrongdoers are in extreme dissension
22|54|And so that those who were given knowledge may know that this [Qur’an] is the truth from your Lord, so they may believe in it and their hearts may become humbled to it. Allah surely guides those who believe to the straight path
22|55|Yet the disbelievers will persist in doubt about it until the Hour comes upon them suddenly or there comes upon them the punishment of a Day devoid of all hope
22|56|The sovereignty on that Day belongs to Allah; He will judge between them, then those who believed and did righteous deeds will be in the Gardens of Bliss
22|57|But those who disbelieve and reject Our verses, for them there will be a humiliating punishment
22|58|As for those who emigrate in the cause of Allah and are killed or died, Allah will surely give them a goodly provision. Indeed, Allah is the Best of Providers
22|59|He will surely admit them to a place that they will be pleased with, and Allah is surely All-Knowing, Most Forbearing
22|60|That is so. Whoever retaliates against an aggressive act with its like and is wronged again, Allah will surely help him. Indeed, Allah is Ever-Pardoning, All-Forgiving
22|61|That is because it is Allah Who causes the night to merge into the day, and causes the day to merge into the night. And Allah is All-Hearing, All-Seeing
22|62|That is because it is Allah Who is the Truth and whatever they invoke besides Him is falsehood, and it is Allah Who is the Most High, the Most Great
22|63|Do you not see that Allah sends down rain from the sky whereupon the earth becomes green? Indeed, Allah is Most Subtle, All-Aware
22|64|To Him belongs all that is in the heavens and all that is on earth, and indeed it is Allah Who is the Self-Sufficient, the Praiseworthy
22|65|Do you not see that Allah has subjected to you all that is on the earth, and the ships that sail through the sea by His command? He holds the sky from falling down on the earth except by His permission. Indeed, Allah is Ever Gracious and Most Merciful to people
22|66|It is He Who gave you life, then will cause you to die, then He will bring you back to life. Indeed, man is ever ungrateful
22|67|For every community We ordained ways of worship which they follow, so do not let them dispute with you [O Prophet] in this matter. But call them to your Lord, for you are indeed on the straight guidance
22|68|And if they argue with you, say, “Allah knows best what you are doing.”
22|69|Allah will judge between you on the Day of Resurrection concerning that over which you used to differ
22|70|Do you not know that Allah knows all that is in the heaven and on earth? That is all [written] in a Record. This is indeed easy for Allah
22|71|Yet they worship other than Allah that for which He has not sent down any authority, and of which they have no knowledge. The wrongdoers will have no helper
22|72|When Our verses are recited to them clearly, you notice disgust on the faces of the disbelievers, as if they are about to attack those who recite Our verses to them. Say, “Shall I inform you of something worse than what you feel at present? It is the Fire! Allah has promised it to those who disbelieve; what a terrible destination
22|73|O people, a similitude is set forth, so listen to it: those whom you invoke besides Allah can never create even a fly, even if they all come together for that. And if a fly snatches something away from them, they cannot retrieve it. How feeble is the invoker as well as the invoked
22|74|They have not revered Allah the reverence He deserves. Indeed, Allah is All-Powerful, All-Mighty
22|75|Allah chooses messengers from the angels and from mankind. Indeed, Allah is All-Hearing, All-Seeing
22|76|He knows all that is ahead of them and all that is behind them, and to Allah returns all matters
22|77|O you who believe, bow down and prostrate, worship Your Lord and do good, so that you may succeed
22|78|Strive in the cause of Allah in a due manner. He has chosen you and has not imposed upon you any hardship in religion – the faith of your father Abraham. He named you as Muslims earlier and in this [Qur’an], so that the Messenger might be a witness over you and you might be witnesses over mankind. So establish prayer, give zakah, and hold fast to Allah, for He is your Protector; what an excellent Protector and an excellent Helper
23|1|The believers have attained true success
23|2|those who humble themselves in their prayers
23|3|and those who turn away from all that is vain
23|4|and those who give zakah
23|5|and those who guard their sexual desires
23|6|except with their wives or slave women they may own, for then they are free of blame
23|7|But whoever seeks anything beyond that, it is they who are the transgressors
23|8|And those who are faithful to their trusts and pledges
23|9|and those who properly observe their prayers
23|10|Such will be the inheritors
23|11|who will inherit Paradise; they will abide therein forever
23|12|We created man from an extract of clay
23|13|then We placed him as a sperm-drop in a safe place
23|14|then We made the sperm-drop into a clinging clot, then We made the clinging clot into a lump, then We made the lump into bones, and We clothed the bones with flesh, and then We developed it into another creation. So Blessed is Allah, the Best of Creators
23|15|Then after that you will surely die
23|16|then on the Day of Resurrection you will surely be resurrected
23|17|We have created above you seven levels [of heaven], and We have never been unaware of Our creation
23|18|We send down water from the sky in due measure and cause it to stay in the earth, and We are surely able to take it away
23|19|With this [water] We produce for you gardens of palm trees and grapevines, in which there are many fruits from which you eat
23|20|and [olive] tree that grows at Mount Sinai, producing oil and condiment for those who eat
23|21|And there is certainly a lesson for you in livestock animals. We provide you with drink out of what they have in their bellies, and for you there are many benefits in them, and from their [meat] you eat
23|22|and on them and on boats you are carried
23|23|We sent Noah to his people. He said, “O my people, worship Allah; you have no god other than Him. Will you not then fear Him?”
23|24|The disbelieving chiefs of his people said, “This is only a man like yourselves who wants to be superior to you. If Allah had willed, He could have sent down angels. We have not heard such a thing from our forefathers
23|25|He is just a madman, so bear with him for a while.”
23|26|Noah said, “My Lord, help me, for they have rejected me.”
23|27|So We inspired him [saying], “Make the Ark under Our Eyes and according to Our directions. Then when Our command comes and the oven bursts with water, take on board a pair of each species and your family, except those against whom the decree has already been passed. And do not plead with Me concerning those who have done wrong, for they will surely be drowned.”
23|28|Then when you and those who are with you have embarked on the Ark, say, “All praise is for Allah, Who saved us from the wrongdoing people.”
23|29|And say: “My Lord, make my landing a blessed landing, for You provide the best landing’”
23|30|Indeed, there are signs in this, and We always put people to test
23|31|Then We raised up after them another generation
23|32|and We sent to them a messenger from among themselves [saying], “Worship Allah; you have no god other than Him. Will you not then fear Him?”
23|33|But the chiefs of his people who disbelieved and denied the meeting of the Hereafter, and whom We had made affluent in the life of this world, said, “He is no more than a man like yourselves; he eats what you eat and drinks what you drink
23|34|If you obey a man like yourselves, you will surely be losers
23|35|Does he promise you that when you have died and become dust and bones, that you will be brought forth
23|36|Far-fetched, utterly far-fetched is what you are promised
23|37|There is nothing except our life of this world; we die, others are born, and none will be resurrected
23|38|He is no more than a man who has fabricated lies about Allah, and we will never believe in him.”
23|39|Noah said, “My Lord, help me for they have rejected me.”
23|40|Allah said, “In a little while they will surely be regretful.”
23|41|So the huge blast overtook them in all justice, and We swept them away like scum. So away with the wrongdoing people
23|42|Then We raised after them other generations
23|43|No nation can bring its appointed time forward, nor can they delay it
23|44|Then We sent Our messengers in succession: every time a messenger came to his people, they rejected him. So We destroyed them, one after the others, and made them mere tales. Away with the people who refuse to believe
23|45|Then We sent Moses and his brother Aaron with Our signs and compelling proof
23|46|to Pharaoh and his chiefs, but they showed arrogance and were haughty people
23|47|They said, “Should we believe in two men like ourselves, when their people are our slaves?”
23|48|So they rejected them both, and were among those who were destroyed
23|49|We gave Moses the Scripture so that they might be guided
23|50|We made the son of Mary and his mother a sign, and sheltered them on a hillside – a place of rest and a flowing stream
23|51|O messengers, eat from the lawful things and act righteously, for I am All-Knowing of what you do
23|52|Indeed, this religion of yours is one religion, and I am your Lord, so fear Me
23|53|But people split up their religion into factions, each faction rejoicing in what it has
23|54|So leave them in their heedlessness for a while
23|55|Do they think that what We give them wealth and children
23|56|that We hasten to them all that is good? No, but they do not perceive it
23|57|Those who are in awe for fearful of their Lord
23|58|and those who believe in the verses of their Lord
23|59|and those who do not associate partners with their Lord
23|60|and those who do whatever [good] they do with their hearts fearful, knowing that they will return to their Lord –
23|61|it is they who hasten to do good deeds, and they are foremost in them
23|62|We do not burden a soul more than what it can bear. We have a Record [of their deeds] that tells the truth, and none will be wronged
23|63|But their hearts are oblivious of this [Qur’an], and they have other [evil] deeds that they are doing
23|64|Until when We seize their affluent ones with punishment, they start crying for help
23|65|“Do not cry for help today, for you will receive no help from Us
23|66|My verses were recited to you, but you used to turn back on your heels
23|67|feeling proud of this [Sacred House], spending night in evil talks [about the Qur’an].”
23|68|Have they not pondered the Words [of Allah], or has there come to them what did not come to their forefathers
23|69|Or is it that they do not recognize their Messenger, so they deny him
23|70|Or do they say, “There is madness in him?” Rather, he has come to them with the truth, but most of them are averse to the truth
23|71|Were the Truth to follow their desires, the heavens and earth, and all those who are therein would have been ruined. In fact, We have given them their Reminder, but they are averse to their Reminder
23|72|Or do you ask them for some reward? But the reward of your Lord is best, and He is the Best of Providers
23|73|Indeed, you are calling them to a straight path
23|74|but those who do not believe in the Hereafter are deviating from that path
23|75|Even if We were to show them mercy and relieve their adversity, they would still persist in their transgression, wandering blindly
23|76|We have already seized them with punishment, but they did not humble themselves to their Lord, nor did they supplicate in humility
23|77|until when We open for them a gateway of a severe punishment, they will be plunged into utter despair
23|78|It is He Who gave you hearing, sight and hearts. How little you give thanks
23|79|And it is He Who spread you on earth, and to Him you will all be gathered
23|80|It is He Who gives life and causes death, and to Him belongs the alternation of night and day. Do you not understand
23|81|But they say the like of what the earlier peoples said
23|82|They say, “Is it that when we die and become dust and bones, will we really be resurrected
23|83|This is what we and our forefathers were promised before; this is nothing but ancient fables.”
23|84|Say, “To whom belong the earth and all those who are on it, if you really know?”
23|85|They will say, “To Allah.” Say, “Will you not then take heed?”
23|86|Say, “Who is the Lord of the seven heavens and the Lord of the Mighty Throne?”
23|87|They will say, “Allah.” Say, “Will you not then fear Him?”
23|88|Say, “In Whose Hand is the dominion of all things – and He gives protection while none can protect against Him – if you really know?”
23|89|They will say, “Allah.” Say, “Then how can you be deluded?”
23|90|In fact, We brought them the truth, but they are certainly liars
23|91|Allah has never begotten a son, nor is there any god besides Him. Otherwise, each god would have taken away what he had created, and each would have tried to gain supremacy over the other. Glory be to Allah far above what they ascribe to Him
23|92|Knower of the unseen and the seen. Exalted is He far above what they associate with Him
23|93|Say, “My Lord, if You show me what they are warned of
23|94|my Lord, then do not include me among the wrongdoing people.”
23|95|We are surely able to show you that of which We have warned them
23|96|Repel evil with what is best; We know well what they claim
23|97|And say, “My Lord, I seek refuge with You from the temptations of the devils
23|98|And I seek refuge with You, my Lord, that they even come near me.”
23|99|Until when death comes to one of them, he says, “My Lord, send me back
23|100|so that I may do righteous deeds in what I left behind.” No, it is only a word he utters. And behind them is a barrier until the Day they are resurrected
23|101|When the Trumpet is blown, there will be no kinship ties between them on that Day, nor will they ask about one another
23|102|So those whose scales [of good deeds] are heavy, it is they who will be successful
23|103|But those whose scales are light, they are the ones who have lost their souls, abiding in Hell forever
23|104|The Fire will scorch their faces, leaving them disfigured
23|105|“Were not My verses recited to you, and you used to reject them?”
23|106|They will say, “Our Lord, our misfortune overwhelmed us, and we were a people who went astray
23|107|Our Lord, take us out of this; if we ever return, we will certainly be wrongdoers.”
23|108|Allah will say, “Stay therein despised, and do not speak to Me
23|109|There was a group of My slaves who used to pray, ‘Our Lord, we believe, so forgive us and have mercy upon us, and You are the Most Merciful of those who show mercy.’
23|110|But you took them in mockery until they made you forget My remembrance, and you used to laugh at them
