23|111|I have rewarded them Today for their patience; it is they who are the successful.”
23|112|He will say, “How many years did you stay on earth?”
23|113|They will say, “We stayed for a day or part of a day; ask those who keep count.”
23|114|Allah will say, “You only stayed for a while, if only you had known
23|115|Did you think that We created you with no purpose, and that you would not be brought back to Us?”
23|116|Exalted is Allah, the True Sovereign! None has the right to be worshiped except Him, the Lord of the Honorable Throne
23|117|Whoever supplicates another god besides Allah, for which he has no proof, his reckoning will be with his Lord. Indeed, the disbelievers will never succeed
23|118|Say, “My Lord, forgive and have mercy, and you are the Best of those who show mercy.”
24|1|[This is] a Chapter which We have sent down and ordained, and sent down in it clear commandments so that you may take heed
24|2|As for the woman and the man who commit fornication; flog each of them a hundred lashes. Do not let pity for them make you lenient concerning the law of Allah, if you believe in Allah and the Last Day. And let a group of the believers witness their punishment
24|3|A man who fornicates would only marry a woman who fornicates or a polytheist, and a woman who fornicates would only marry a man who fornicates or a polytheist. Such marriages are forbidden to the believers
24|4|As for those who accuse chaste women [of adultery] but fail to produce four witnesses, flog them eighty lashes and do not accept their testimony ever, for it is they who are the rebellious
24|5|except those who repent afterwards and mend their ways, for Allah is All-Forgiving, Most Merciful
24|6|As for those who accuse their wives [of adultery] but have no witness except themselves, then the evidence of one of them is to testify four times by Allah that he is telling the truth
24|7|and the fifth [oath] is that may Allah curse him if he is telling a lie
24|8|But she will be spared the punishment if she testifies four times by Allah that he is telling a lie
24|9|and the fifth [oath] is that may Allah’s wrath be upon her if he is telling the truth
24|10|Were it not for Allah’s grace and mercy upon you, and that Allah is Accepting of Repentance, All-Wise, [He would have punished you]
24|11|Indeed, those who came up with the slander are a group among you. Do not think that it is bad for you, rather it is good for you. Each one of them is responsible for what he earned of the sin, and the one who played the major role, for him there will be a grave punishment
24|12|If only the believing men and women had thought well of themselves, and said, “This is a clear slander!”
24|13|Why did they not produce four witnesses to prove it? Now, since they failed to produce witnesses, they are the liars before Allah
24|14|Were it not for Allah’s grace and mercy upon you in this world and in the Hereafter, you would have been afflicted with a great punishment for that [lie] in which you were involved
24|15|when you were passing it from one tongue to the other, and saying with your mouths what you had no knowledge of, and were taking it lightly, whereas with Allah it was a grave offense
24|16|If only you had said when you heard it, “How can we speak about such a thing! Glory be to You [O Allah]! This is a monstrous slander!”
24|17|Allah admonishes you not to repeat such a thing ever, if you are [truly] believers
24|18|Allah makes the revelations clear to you, for Allah is All-Knowing, All-Wise
24|19|Indeed, those who like to see indecency spread among the believers will have a painful punishment in this world and the Hereafter; Allah knows and you do not know
24|20|Were it not for Allah’s grace and mercy upon you, and that Allah is Ever Gracious, Most Merciful [He would have punished you]
24|21|O you who believe, do not follow the footsteps of Satan; whoever follows the footsteps of Satan, he only enjoins indecency and evil acts. Were it not for Allah’s grace and mercy upon you, none of you would have ever been purified. But Allah purifies whom He wills, and Allah is All-Hearing, All-Knowing
24|22|The people of virtue and affluence among you should not swear to withhold their aid from their relatives, the needy and the emigrants in the cause of Allah. Let them pardon and overlook. Do you not like to be forgiven by Allah? For Allah is All-Forgiving, Most Merciful
24|23|Those who [falsely] accuse chaste, innocent and believing women are cursed in this life and the Hereafter, and for them there will be a great punishment
24|24|On the Day when their tongues, hands and feet will testify against them for what they used to do
24|25|On that Day, Allah will give them full recompense that they deserve, and they will know that it is Allah Who is the Ultimate Truth
24|26|Evil women are for evil men and evil men for evil women, and virtuous women are for virtuous men and virtuous men for virtuous women. These [virtuous ones] are innocent of what [the slanderers] say; they will have forgiveness and a generous provision
24|27|O you who believe, do not enter any house other than your own until you ask permission and greet their dwellers. That is best for you, so that you may take heed
24|28|If you do not find anyone therein, do not enter it until you have been given permission. If you are told to go back, then go back; that is more proper for you. And Allah is All-Knowing of what you do
24|29|There is no blame on you if you enter uninhabited houses with a useful purpose. And Allah knows what you reveal and what you conceal
24|30|Tell the believing men to lower their gazes and guard their private parts; that is purer for them. Indeed, Allah is All-Aware of what they do
24|31|Tell the believing women to lower their gazes and guard their private parts, and not to reveal their beauty except what appears. And let them draw their veils over their chests, and not to reveal their beauty except to their husbands, their fathers, their fathers-in-law, their sons, their stepsons, their brothers, their brothers’ sons or sisters’ sons, their fellow women, slaves whom they own, male attendants who have no [sexual] desire, or children who are still unaware of private aspects of women. Nor let them stamp their feet in order to draw attention to their hidden charm. And turn to Allah in repentance all together, O believers, so that you may be successful
24|32|Arrange marriages for those of you who are unmarried, and for the righteous of your bondmen and bondwomen. If they are poor, Allah will suffice them from His bounty, for Allah is All-Bountiful, All-Knowing
24|33|Let those who cannot afford marriage to keep themselves chaste until Allah suffices them from His bounty. If any of your slaves wish to enter the contract of emancipation, make this contract with them, if you find goodness in them, and give them some of the wealth that Allah has given you. Do not compel your slave girls into prostitution – if they wish to keep chaste – seeking the worldly gains of this life. But if anyone compels them, then Allah, after such a compulsion, is All-Forgiving, Most Merciful
24|34|We have sent down to you verses clarifying the right path, and examples of those who passed on before you, and an admonition for those who fear Allah
24|35|Allah is the Light of the heavens and earth. The likeness of His light is that of a niche in which is a lamp; the lamp is in a glass; the glass is like a shining star – it is lit by [the oil of] a blessed olive tree, which is neither of the east nor of the west. Its oil would almost glow, even without being touched by fire. Light upon light; Allah guides to His light whom He wills. Allah sets forth comparisons for people, and Allah is All-Knowing of everything
24|36|[Such niches are lit] in the houses [of worship] which Allah has ordered to raise up, and where His Name is mentioned, and He is glorified therein morning and evening
24|37|by men who are not distracted by buying or selling from the remembrance of Allah, or from performing prayer or giving zakah. They fear a Day when hearts and eyes will be petrified
24|38|[They hope] that Allah may reward them according to their best deeds, and give them yet more out of His bounty, for Allah gives provision to whom He wills without limit
24|39|As for those who disbelieve, their deeds are like a mirage in a plain desert, which a thirsty person deems to be water, until when he reaches it, he finds nothing, but he finds Allah there [in the Hereafter], thus He will pay him his account in full, for Allah is swift in reckoning
24|40|Or [their deeds] are like layers of darkness in a deep sea covered by waves upon waves, above which are clouds - layers of darkness, one above another. If one stretches out his hand, he can hardly see it. Whoever Allah does not give light will have no light at all
24|41|Do you not see that all those who are in the heavens and earth glorify Allah, as do the birds with wings outspread? Each knows its [way of] praying and glorification. And Allah is All-Knowing of what they do
24|42|To Allah belongs the dominion of the heavens and earth, and to Allah is the final return
24|43|Do you not see that Allah drives the clouds, then gathers them together, then turns them into a heap, then you see raindrops coming out from their midst? He sends down hail from mountains [of clouds] in the sky, raining it down upon whoever He wills and turning it away from whoever He wills. The flash of its lightning almost takes away eyesight
24|44|Allah alternates the night and day. Indeed, there is a lesson in this for people of insight
24|45|Allah created every living creature from water. Some of them move on their bellies, and some walk on two legs and some walk on four. Allah creates what He wills. Allah is Most Capable of all things
24|46|We have sent down verses making things clear, and Allah guides whom He wills to a straight path
24|47|They [the hypocrites] say, “We believe in Allah and in the Messenger, and we obey.” Then a party of them turns away after that. Such are not believers
24|48|When they are called to Allah and His Messenger so that he may judge between them, a party of them turns away
24|49|But if the right is in their favor, they come to him in full submission
24|50|Is there sickness in their hearts, or do they have doubt, or do they fear that Allah and His messenger will be unjust to them? Rather, it is they who are the wrongdoers
24|51|As for the believers, when they are called to Allah and His Messenger so that he may judge between them, they say, “We listen and obey.” It is they who are the successful
24|52|Whoever obeys Allah and His Messenger, and fears Allah and is conscious of Him – it is they who are the triumphant
24|53|They [the hypocrites] swear by Allah their most solemn oaths that if you order them, they will surely march forth. Say, “do not swear, [your] obedience is well known. Allah is All-Aware of what you do.”
24|54|Say, “Obey Allah and obey the Messenger. But if you turn away, he is only responsible for his duty and you are responsible for your duty. If you obey him, you will be guided. The duty of the Messenger is only to convey the message clearly.”
24|55|Allah has promised those among you who believe and do righteous deeds that He will make them successors in the land, as He made those who came before them, and He will surely establish for them their religion which He has chosen for them, and He will surely change their state of fear into security; that they worship Me, not associating anything with Me. But whoever disbelieves after that, it is they who are the rebellious
24|56|Establish prayer, give zakah and obey the Messenger, so that you may be shown mercy
24|57|Do not think that the disbelievers can escape in the land. Their abode will be the Fire. What a terrible destination
24|58|O you who believe, let your slaves and those among you who have not reached puberty ask for your permission [to enter] at three times: before dawn prayer, when you take off your outer garments at noon, and after the night prayer; three times of privacy for you. Beyond that there is no blame on you nor on them to move about freely, attending to one another. This is how Allah makes the verses clear to you, for Allah is All-Knowing, All-Wise
24|59|When your children reach the age of puberty, let them ask permission [to enter], as their elders do. This is how Allah makes His verses clear to you, for Allah is All-Knowing, All-Wise
24|60|As for elderly women who have no interest in marriage, there is no blame on them if they take off their outer garments without revealing their beauty. But if they modestly refrain from it, that is better for them. And Allah is All-Hearing, All-Knowing
24|61|There is no blame on a blind person, nor on the lame, nor on the sick, nor on yourselves if you eat from your houses or from your fathers’ houses or your mothers’ houses or your brothers’ houses or your sisters’ houses or your paternal uncles’ houses, or your paternal aunts’ houses or your maternal uncles’ houses or your maternal aunts’ houses or from the houses the keys of which are in your possession, or your friends’ houses. There is no blame on you if you eat together or separately. But when you enter houses, greet one another with greetings of peace from Allah, which is blessed and delightful. This is how Allah makes the verses clear to you, so that you may understand
24|62|The true believers are those who believe in Allah and His Messenger. When they are with him on a public matter, they do not leave until they ask his permission. Those who ask your permission are the ones who believe in Allah and His Messenger. So when they ask your permission for a private matter, give permission to whom you will from among them, and ask Allah’s forgiveness for them, for Allah is All-Forgiving, Most Merciful
24|63|Do not consider the Messenger’s summons to you as your summons to one another. Allah surely knows those of you who slip away hiding behind others. So let those who disobey his command beware lest some trial may afflict them or they may be afflicted with a painful punishment
24|64|Surely to Allah belongs all that is in the heavens and earth. He knows all what you do. On the Day they return to Him, He will inform them of what they did. And Allah is All-Knowing of everything
25|1|Blessed is the One Who has sent down the Criterion to His slave, so that he may be a warner to the worlds
25|2|He to Whom belongs the dominion of the heavens and earth, Who has never begotten a son, and has no partner in His dominion. He has created everything and measured it precisely
25|3|They have taken besides Him other gods who can create nothing but are themselves created. Nor do they have power to harm or benefit themselves, nor do they have power to cause death, give life or resurrect the dead
25|4|Those who disbelieve say, “This [Qur’an] is nothing but a lie which he has fabricated, with the help of other people.” What they claim is totally unjust and false
25|5|And they say, “Ancient fables which he has written down; they are dictated to him morning and evening.”
25|6|Say, “It has been sent down by the One Who knows the secrets of the heavens and earth. He is All-Forgiving, Most Merciful.”
25|7|And they say, “What kind of messenger is this who eats food and walks in the markets? If only an angel had been sent down to him to be a warner with him
25|8|or a treasure had been cast down to him, or he had a garden to eat from it.” The wrongdoers say, “You are following none but a bewitched man.”
25|9|See how they call you names. Thus they have gone astray and cannot find a way
25|10|Blessed is He Who, if He wills, could give you better than that: gardens under which rivers flow, and could give you palaces
25|11|But they deny the Hour, and We have prepared for those who deny the Hour a Blazing Fire
25|12|When it sees them from a far distance, they will hear its raging and roaring
25|13|And when they are thrown into a narrow space therein, chained together, they will cry out for death
25|14|Do not cry out this Day for death only once, but cry out many times.”
25|15|Say, “Is that better or the Eternal Paradise which has been promised to the righteous?” It will be as a reward for them and as a final destination
25|16|They will have there whatever they wish for, abiding therein forever. That is a promise that your Lord has taken upon Himself.”
25|17|On the Day when He will gather them along with those whom they worshiped besides Allah, He will say, “Did you mislead these slaves of Mine, or did they stray from the right way on their own?”
25|18|They will say, “Glory be to You! It was not for us to take besides You any guardians. But You provided for them and their forefathers pleasures, until they forgot the message, for they were a ruined people.”
25|19|Thus they [the idols] will deny all what you say, so you cannot avert [punishment] nor can get any help. Whoever among you does wrong, We will make him taste a great punishment
25|20|We did not send any messengers before you [O Prophet] except that they ate food and walked in the markets. We have made some of you as a trial for others. Will you have patience? For your Lord is All-Seeing
25|21|Those who do not expect to meet Us say, “Why are angels not sent down to us or why do we not see our Lord?” They have been too proud of themselves, and have transgressed immensely
25|22|On the Day when they see the angels, there will be no glad tidings for the wicked, and [the angels] will say, “Absolutely forbidden for you.”
25|23|We will turn to whatever deeds they did and turn them into scattered dust
25|24|On that Day the people of Paradise will have the best abode and the finest resting place
25|25|On the Day when the sky will split asunder with clouds, and the angels will be sent down in succession
25|26|The true dominion on that Day belongs to the Most Compassionate, and it will be a hard day for the disbelievers
25|27|On that Day, the wrongdoer will bite his hands saying, “Would that I had taken a way with the Messenger
25|28|Woe to me! Would that I had not taken so-and-so as a close friend
25|29|He led me astray from the Reminder after it had come to me.” Satan always betrays man
25|30|The Messenger said, “O my Lord, my people have taken this Qur’an as a thing to be abandoned.”
25|31|Thus did we assign for every prophet an enemy from among the wicked, but your Lord is sufficient as a Guide and Helper
25|32|Those who disbelieve say, “Why was the Qur’an not sent down to him all at once?” [We sent it] in this way so that We may strengthen your heart thereby, and We have revealed it in a gradual manner
25|33|Whenever they bring you an argument, We bring you the truth and the best explanation
25|34|Those who will be dragged on their faces to Hell – they will be in the worst position and farthest astray from the right path
25|35|We gave Moses the Scripture and appointed with him his brother Aaron as a helper
25|36|We said, “Go, both of you, to the people who have rejected Our signs.” Then We destroyed them utterly
25|37|Also the people of Noah, when they rejected the messengers, We drowned them and made them an example for mankind. And We have prepared for the wrongdoers a painful punishment
25|38|Also [We destroyed] ‘Ād and Thamūd, and the people of the Well, and many generations between them
25|39|To each We gave examples [of the previous nations], and each We destroyed completely
25|40|They have surely passed by the town that was destroyed by a terrible rain [of stones]. Have they not seen it? But they do not expect to be resurrected
25|41|When they see you [O Prophet], they only ridicule you, “Is this the one whom Allah has sent as a messenger
25|42|He would have almost led us astray from our gods, if we had not been so devoted to them.” But when they see the punishment, they will come to know who is further astray from the right way
25|43|Have you [O Prophet] seen the one who takes his desire as his god, will you then be a keeper over him
25|44|Do you think that most of them hear or understand? They are just like livestock, rather they are further astray from the right way
25|45|Do you not see how your Lord extends the shade? If He had willed, He could have made it still. Then We made the sun an indication for it
25|46|Then We gradually draw it towards Us [as the sun climbs up]
25|47|It is He Who has made the night as a garment for you, and made sleep for rest; and has made daytime for returning to life
25|48|It is He Who sends the winds as harbingers before His mercy, and We send down from the sky pure water
25|49|so that We may revive therewith a dead land, and quench the thirst of countless beasts and humans We have created
25|50|We distribute it among them so that they may take heed, but most people persist in their ingratitude
25|51|If We had willed, We could have sent to each town a warner
25|52|So do not obey the disbelievers, but strive against them with this [Qur’an] a great striving
25|53|It is He Who merges the two bodies of water: one fresh and palatable and the other salty and bitter, and He has made between them a barrier and an insurmountable partition
25|54|It is He Who created human beings from water, then made between them bonds of kinship and marriage, for your Lord is Most Capable
25|55|Yet they worship besides Allah that which can neither benefit nor harm them; the disbeliever always collaborates against his Lord
25|56|We have not sent you [O Prophet] except as a bearer of glad tidings and a warner
25|57|Say, “I do not ask you for any reward for it, except that anyone who wishes to take a path to his Lord.”
25|58|Put your trust in the Ever-Living Who never dies, and glorify Him with praise. He is Sufficient as All-Aware of the sins of His slaves –
25|59|it is He Who created the heavens and earth and all that is between them in six Days, then rose over the Throne. He is the Most Compassionate, so ask about Him the One Who is All-Aware
25|60|When it is said to them, “Prostrate to the Most Compassionate,” they say, “What is ‘the Most Compassionate?’ Shall we prostrate to what you order us?” And it only increases them in aversion
25|61|Blessed is He Who placed in the sky constellations, and placed therein a radiant lamp and a luminous moon
25|62|It is He Who made the night and the day to follow each other so that everyone who wishes may reflect or become grateful
25|63|The slaves of the Most Compassionate are those who walk on earth humbly, and when the ignorant address them, they only say words of peace
25|64|and those who spend the night prostrating and standing before their Lord
25|65|and those who say, “Our Lord, turn the punishment of Hell away from us, for its punishment is unrelenting.”
25|66|It is an evil place to settle and an evil abode.”
25|67|And those who neither spend wastefully nor stingily, but are moderate between them
25|68|and those who do not invoke besides Allah another god, and who do not kill a soul whom Allah has forbidden, except in the course of justice, and who do not commit adultery, for whoever does any of this will face the penalty
25|69|the punishment will be doubled for him on the Day of Resurrection, wherein he will remain disgraced forever
25|70|except those who repent and believe, and do righteous deeds; for them Allah will change their evil deeds into good deeds, for Allah is All-Forgiving, Most Merciful
25|71|Whoever repents and does righteous deeds has turned to Allah with sincere repentance
25|72|And those who do not witness falsehood, and when they pass by futility, they pass by with dignity
25|73|and those who, when they are reminded with the verses of their Lord, they do not turn a deaf ear or a blind eye to them
25|74|and those who say, “Our Lord, let our spouses and children be a source of joy for us, and make us good examples for the righteous.”
25|75|It is they who will be rewarded with high palaces [in Paradise] for their perseverance, and they will be received therein with salutations and greetings of peace
25|76|abiding therein forever. What an excellent abode and a resting place
25|77|Say [O Prophet], “My Lord would not care at all about you, were it not for your supplication. Now since you have rejected [the truth], the inevitable is bound to come.”
26|1|Tā sīn mīm
26|2|These are the verses of the clear Book
26|3|Perhaps you will grieve yourself to death because they do not believe
26|4|If We willed, We could send down upon them a sign from the heaven, at which their necks would stay bowed in humility
26|5|No new reminder comes to them from the Most Compassionate except that they turn away from it
26|6|They have rejected [the Truth], soon there will come to them the consequences of their ridicule
26|7|Do they not see the earth, how many fine kinds of plants We grow in it
26|8|Indeed, there is a sign in this, yet most of them will not believe
26|9|Your Lord is indeed the All-Mighty, the Most Merciful
26|10|And [remember] when your Lord called out to Moses, “Go to the wrongdoing people –
26|11|the people of Pharaoh; will they not fear [the punishment of] Allah?”
26|12|He said, “My Lord, I fear that they may reject me
26|13|and I will feel distressed and my tongue will not be fluent, so send Aaron along [to help me]
26|14|Moreover, they have a charge against me, so I fear they may kill me.”
26|15|Allah said, “Certainly not! Go, both of you, with Our signs; We are with you, listening
26|16|Go to Pharaoh and say, ‘We are the messengers from the Lord of the worlds
26|17|that you let the Children of Israel go with us.’”
26|18|Pharaoh said, “Did we not bring you up as a child among us, and you stayed with us several years of your life
26|19|Yet you did what you did, and you are extremely ungrateful.”
26|20|He said, “I did it when I had no guidance
26|21|So I fled from you in fear. Then my Lord gave me wisdom and made me one of the messengers
26|22|Is this a favor that you remind me with, that you have enslaved the Children of Israel
26|23|Pharaoh said, “What is ‘the Lord of the worlds’?”
26|24|Moses said, “The Lord of the heavens and earth and all that is between them, if only you had sure faith.”
26|25|Pharaoh said to those around him, “Did you hear [what he just said]?”
26|26|Moses said, “Your Lord and the Lord of your forefathers.”
26|27|Pharaoh said, “Your messenger who has been sent to you is truly insane!”
26|28|Moses said, “Lord of the east and west and all that is between them, if only you had sense!”
26|29|Pharaoh said, “If you take any god other than me, I will throw you into prison.”
26|30|Moses said, “What if I bring you a clear proof?”
26|31|Pharaoh said, “Bring it then, if you are truthful!”
26|32|So he threw down his staff, and suddenly it was a real serpent
26|33|And he drew out his hand, and it was glowing white to the beholders
26|34|Pharaoh said to the chiefs around him, “This is indeed a learned magician
26|35|He wants to drive you out of your land with his magic. What do you suggest?”
26|36|They said, “Let him and his brother wait and dispatch heralds to the cities
26|37|to bring you every learned magician.”
26|38|So the magician were assembled at an appointed time on a known day
26|39|And it was said to the people, “Will you join the gathering
26|40|so that we may follow the magicians if they are victorious?”
26|41|When the magicians came, they said to Pharaoh, “Will there be a reward for us if we are victorious?”
26|42|He said, “Yes, and then you will surely be of those who are close to me.”
26|43|Moses said to them, “Throw whatever you wish to throw.”
26|44|So they threw their ropes and staffs, and said, “By the glory of Pharaoh, it is we who will be the victorious!”
26|45|Then Moses threw his staff, and at once it swallowed up all objects of their illusion
26|46|So the magicians fell down in prostration
26|47|They said, “We believe in the Lord of the worlds
26|48|the Lord of Moses and Aaron.”
26|49|Pharaoh said, “How dare you believe in him before I give you permission. Indeed, he is your master who taught you magic, but you will soon come to know. I will surely cut off your hands and feet on opposite sides, then I will crucify you all.”
26|50|They said, “No harm; we will surely return to our Lord
26|51|We hope that our Lord will forgive us our sins, as we are the first of the believers.”
26|52|We inspired Moses, “Leave with My slaves by night; you will surely be pursued.”
26|53|So Pharaoh sent heralds to the cities
26|54|saying, “These are but a small band
26|55|and they have enraged us
26|56|but we are all well-prepared.”
26|57|Thus did We drive them out of their gardens and springs
26|58|and their treasures and splendid dwellings
26|59|So it was; and We made the Children of Israel to inherit them
26|60|They pursued them at sunrise
26|61|When the two groups saw each other, the companions of Moses said, “We are surely overtaken!”
26|62|Moses said, “Certainly not! My Lord is with me; He will guide me.”
26|63|Then We inspired Moses, “Strike the sea with your staff,” so it parted, each part became like a huge mountain
26|64|Then We brought the others [pursuers] close to that place
26|65|and We saved Moses and all those who were with him
26|66|then We drowned the others
26|67|Indeed, there is a sign in this, yet most of them would not believe
26|68|Indeed, your Lord is the All-Mighty, the Most Merciful
26|69|Relate to them the story of Abraham
26|70|when he said to his father and his people, “What do you worship?”
26|71|They said, “We worship idols and remain devoted to them.”
26|72|He said, “Do they hear you when you call upon them
26|73|Or can they benefit or harm you?”
26|74|They said, “No, but this is what we found our forefathers doing.”
26|75|He said, “Do you see what you have been worshiping
26|76|you and your ancestors
26|77|Indeed, they are my enemies, except the Lord of the worlds
26|78|Who created me, so He guides me
26|79|and it is He Who provides me with food and drink
26|80|and when I am ill He heals me
26|81|and He will cause me to die then bring me back to life
26|82|and I hope that He will forgive me my sins on the Day of Judgment.”
26|83|“My Lord, grant me knowledge, and join me with the righteous
26|84|and grant me an honorable mention among the later generations
26|85|and make me of those who will inherit the Garden of Bliss
26|86|and forgive my father, for he is one of those who have gone astray
26|87|and do not disgrace me on the Day when all will be resurrected –
26|88|the Day when neither wealth nor children will be of any avail
26|89|except the one who comes to Allah with a sound heart.”
26|90|Paradise will be brought near to the righteous
26|91|and Hellfire will be uncovered to those who went astray
26|92|and they will be told, “Where are those whom you used to worship
26|93|other than Allah? Can they help you or even help themselves?”
26|94|Then they will be hurled into Hell one upon another, along with those who led them astray
26|95|and the followers of Iblīs, all together
26|96|There the deviants will say while quarreling with their false deities
26|97|“By Allah, we were clearly misguided
26|98|when we deemed you equal to the Lord of the worlds
26|99|None led us astray except the wicked
26|100|Now we neither have any intercessors
26|101|nor a close friend
26|102|If only we had a chance to return, we would be among the believers.”
26|103|Indeed, there is a sign in this, yet most of them would not believe
26|104|Your Lord is surely the All-Mighty, the Most Merciful
26|105|The people of Noah rejected the messengers
26|106|when their brother Noah said to them, “Do you not fear Allah
26|107|I am a trustworthy messenger to you
26|108|so fear Allah, and obey me
26|109|I seek of you no reward for this; my reward is only with the Lord of the worlds
26|110|so fear Allah, and obey me.”
26|111|They said, “Shall we believe in you when you are followed by the lowest people?”
26|112|He said, “What knowledge do I have of what they do
26|113|Their reckoning is only with my Lord, if you realize
26|114|I am not going to drive the believers away
26|115|I am only a clear warner.”
26|116|They said, “O Noah, if you do not desist, you will certainly be stoned.”
26|117|He said, “My Lord, my people have rejected me
26|118|So judge between me and them decisively, and save me and the believers who are with me.”
26|119|So We saved him and those who were with him in the fully laden Ark
26|120|Then We drowned thereafter all the rest
26|121|Indeed, there is a sign in this, yet most of them would not believe
26|122|Indeed, your Lord is the All-Mighty, the Most Merciful
26|123|The people of ‘Ād rejected the messengers
26|124|when their brother Hūd said to them, “Will you not fear Allah
26|125|I am a trustworthy messenger to you
26|126|so fear Allah, and obey me
26|127|I do not ask you for any reward for this; my reward is only with the Lord of the worlds
26|128|Do you build a landmark on every high place for no purpose
26|129|And do you construct for yourselves palaces, hoping that you will live forever
26|130|And when you attack [others], do you attack ruthlessly
26|131|So fear Allah, and obey me
26|132|And fear the One Who has provided you with everything you know
26|133|Who provided you with livestock and children
26|134|and with gardens and springs
26|135|I fear for you the punishment of a momentous day.”
26|136|They said, “It is the same to us whether you admonish us or not
26|137|This is nothing but the custom of the former people
26|138|and we will never be punished.”
26|139|Thus they rejected him, so We destroyed them. Indeed, there is a sign in this, yet most of them would not believe
26|140|Your Lord is indeed the All-Mighty, the Most Merciful
26|141|The people of Thamūd rejected the messengers
26|142|when their brother Sālih said to them, “Will you not fear Allah
26|143|I am a trustworthy messenger to you
26|144|so fear Allah, and obey me
26|145|I do not ask you for any reward for this; my reward is only with the Lord of the worlds
26|146|Will you be left secure in whatever you have here
26|147|in gardens and springs
26|148|and in fields of crops and date-palms laden with tender fruit
26|149|carving out houses in the mountains with great skill
26|150|So fear Allah, and obey me
26|151|And do not obey the command of the transgressors
26|152|those who spread corruption in the land and never do what is right.”
26|153|They said, “You are but one of those who are bewitched
26|154|You are but a human like us, so bring a sign if you are one of the truthful.”
26|155|Sālih said, “This is a she-camel; she will have her share of water and you will have yours, each on a specified day
26|156|Do not touch her with harm, or you will be seized by the punishment of a horrible day.”
26|157|But they hamstrung her, then they became regretful
26|158|So the punishment seized them. Indeed, there is a sign in this, yet most of them would not believe
26|159|Your Lord is indeed the All-Mighty, the Most Merciful
26|160|The people of Lot rejected the messengers
26|161|when their brother Lot said to them, “Will you not fear Allah
26|162|I am a trustworthy messenger to you
26|163|so fear Allah, and obey me
26|164|I do not ask you for any reward for this; my reward is only with the Lord of the worlds
26|165|Do you approach males with lust among all people
26|166|leaving the wives whom your Lord has created for you? You are but a transgressing people.”
26|167|They said, “O Lot, If you do not desist, you will surely be expelled.”
26|168|Lot said, “I utterly abhor your practice
26|169|My Lord, save me and my family from [the consequences of] what they do.”
26|170|So We saved him and all his family
26|171|except an old woman who was among those who remained behind
26|172|Then We destroyed the rest
26|173|and We poured down upon them a rain [of stones]. How terrible was the rain of those who were warned
26|174|Indeed, there is a sign in this, yet most of them would not believe
26|175|Your Lord is indeed the All-Mighty, the Most Merciful
26|176|The people of the Forest rejected the messengers
26|177|When Shu‘ayb said to them, “Will you not fear Allah
26|178|I am a trustworthy messenger to you
26|179|so fear Allah, and obey me
26|180|I do not ask you for any reward for this; my reward is only with the Lord of the worlds
26|181|Give full measure and do not be of those who defraud others
26|182|and weigh with accurate scales
26|183|and do not defraud people of their goods, nor go about in the land spreading corruption
26|184|And fear the One Who created you and the former peoples.”
26|185|They said, “You are truly bewitched
26|186|You are only a human being like us, and we think you are nothing but a liar
26|187|So cause pieces of the sky to fall upon us, if you are of the truthful.”
26|188|Shu‘ayb said, “My Lord knows best whatever you do.”
26|189|Thus they rejected him, so they were seized by the punishment of the cloudy day; it was the punishment of a horrible day
26|190|Indeed, there is a sign in this, yet most of them would not believe
26|191|Your Lord is indeed the All-Mighty, the Most Merciful
26|192|This is indeed a revelation from the Lord of the worlds
26|193|which the Trustworthy Spirit [Gabriel] has brought down
26|194|to your heart [O Prophet] so that you may be one of the warners
26|195|in clear Arabic language
26|196|And it was indeed [mentioned] in the scriptures of the former peoples
26|197|Was it not a proof for them that the learned men of the Children of Israel recognized it [to be true]
26|198|If We had sent it down to any of the non-Arabs
26|199|and he had recited it to them, still they would not have believed in it
26|200|This is how We made it [disbelief] enter the hearts of the wicked
26|201|They will not believe in it until they see the painful punishment
26|202|which will come upon them suddenly when they least expect it
26|203|They will then say, “Can we be granted some respite?”
26|204|Do they really seek to hasten Our punishment
26|205|Tell me [O Prophet] if We give them a life of ease for years
26|206|then there came to them what they were warned of
26|207|what would avail them the life of ease that they were given
26|208|We never destroyed any town without sending them warners
26|209|to admonish them, for We are never unjust
26|210|This [Qur’an] is not sent down by the devils
26|211|it is not for them to do this, nor is it within their capability
26|212|for they are strictly barred from overhearing it
26|213|So do not call upon any other god besides Allah, lest you become of those who will be punished
26|214|And warn [starting with] the nearest kinsfolk
26|215|and lower your wing [in kindness] to the believers who follow you
26|216|But if they disobey you, say, “I disown what you do.”
26|217|And put your trust in the All-Mighty, the Most Merciful
26|218|Who sees you when you stand up [for prayer]
26|219|and your movements among those who prostrate
26|220|Indeed, He is the All-Hearing, the All-Knowing
26|221|Shall I inform you upon who the devils descend
26|222|They descend upon every sinful liar
26|223|who whisper hearsay in the ears, but most of them are liars
26|224|As for poets, they are followed by the deviants
26|225|Do you not see that they wander aimlessly in every valley
26|226|and that they say what they do not do
26|227|Except those who believe, do righteous deeds, remember Allah much and defend themselves after being wronged. The wrongdoers will come to know what end awaits them
27|1|Tā Sīn. These are the verses of the Qur’an and a clear book
27|2|a guidance and glad tidings for the believers
27|3|those who establish prayer and give zakah, and who firmly believe in the Hereafter
27|4|As for those who do not believe in the Hereafter, We have made their deeds appealing to them, so they wander blindly
27|5|Such are those who will have a terrible punishment, and it is they who will be the greatest losers in the Hereafter
27|6|Indeed, you are receiving the Qur’an from the All-Wise, All-Knowing
27|7|[Remember] when Moses said to his family, “I have spotted a fire. I will bring you some news from there, or bring you a burning brand so that you may warm yourselves.”
27|8|When he came to it, he was called, “Blessed is He Who is at the fire and those who are around it. Glory be to Allah, the Lord of the worlds
27|9|O Moses, verily this is Me – Allah, the All-Mighty, the All-Wise
27|10|Throw down your staff!” But when he saw it slithering as if it were a snake, he turned and ran away without looking back. “O Moses, do not be afraid! Indeed, the messengers should have no fear in My presence
27|11|except he who does wrong, then substitutes good for evil, then I am indeed All-Forgiving, Most Merciful
27|12|Put your hand into your garment, it will come out shining white without blemish, as one of nine signs to Pharaoh and his people, for they are indeed a rebellious people.”
27|13|But when Our visible signs came to them, they said, “This is clear magic.”
27|14|They denied them wrongfully and arrogantly, although their hearts were convinced that they were true. See then how was the end of those who spread corruption
27|15|We gave David and Solomon knowledge, and they said, “All praise be to Allah, Who has favored us over many of His believing slaves.”
27|16|Solomon succeeded David, and said, “O people, we have been taught the speech of birds, and we have been given from all things. This is indeed a clear favor.”
27|17|Solomon’s armies of jinn, men and birds were assembled before him, marching in organized ranks
27|18|until when they reached a valley of the ants, an ant said, “O ants, get into your dwellings, so Solomon and his armies do not crush you unknowingly.”
27|19|So he smiled in amusement at her words and said, “My Lord, inspire me to be grateful for Your favor which You have bestowed upon me and my parents, and to do righteous deeds that please you. And admit me, by Your mercy, among Your righteous slaves.”
27|20|Once he checked the birds, and said, “Why is it that I do not see the hoopoe – or is he among the absent
27|21|I will surely punish him severely, or slaughter him, unless he brings me a valid reason.”
27|22|It was not long before the hoopoe came and said, “I have learned something that you do not; I come to you from Sheba with sure news
27|23|I found a woman ruling over them, who has been given of all things, and she has a great throne
27|24|I found her and her people prostrating before the sun instead of Allah. Satan has made their deeds appealing to them and turned them away from the right way, so they are not guided
27|25|so that they do not prostrate before Allah Who brings forth what is hidden in the heavens and earth, and Who knows all that you conceal and all that you reveal
27|26|Allah; none has the right to be worshiped except Him, the Lord of the Mighty Throne.”
27|27|Solomon said, “We will see whether you have told the truth or you are one of the liars
27|28|Take this letter of mine and deliver it to them, then withdraw and see how they respond.”
27|29|The Queen said, “O chiefs, a noble letter has been delivered to me
27|30|It is from Solomon, and it reads, ‘In the name of Allah, the Most Compassionate, the Most Merciful
27|31|Do not be arrogant towards me, but come to me in full submission.”
27|32|She said, “O chiefs, advice me in this matter of mine, for I would make no decision without your consent.”
27|33|They said, “We are powerful and great fighters, but the decision is yours, so consider what you will command.”
27|34|She said, “When kings enter a town, they ravage it and humiliate its notables; this is what they really do
27|35|But I will send them a gift, then see with what response the envoys will return.”
27|36|When the envoy came to Solomon, he said, “Do you seek to appease me with wealth? What Allah has given me is far better than what He has given you. Rather, it is you who take pleasure in gifts
27|37|Go back to them; we will surely come to them with forces that they cannot resist, and we will surely drive them out therefrom in disgrace, fully humbled.”
27|38|He said, “O chiefs, which one of you can bring me her throne before they come to me in submission?”
27|39|A powerful jinn said, “I will bring it to you before you rise up from your council, and I am strong enough and trustworthy.”
27|40|But the one who had some knowledge of the scripture said, “I will bring it to you in the blink of your eye.” When he saw it placed before him, he said, “This is a favor of my Lord, to test me whether I will be grateful or ungrateful. Whoever is grateful, it is only for his own good; and whoever is ungrateful, then my Lord is Self-Sufficient, Most Generous.”
27|41|He said, “Disguise her throne for her, so we may see whether she can discover the truth, or she will be of those who cannot recognize.”
27|42|So when she came, she was asked, “Is your throne like this?” She said, “It looks as if it is the same. We were given knowledge beforehand, and have submitted [to Allah].”
27|43|But she was hindered [from the faith] because she used to worship other than Allah, for she came from a disbelieving people
27|44|It was said to her, “Enter the palace.” But when she saw it, she thought it was a body of water, so she uncovered her calves. He said, “This is a palace paved with crystal.” She said, “My Lord, I have wronged myself, and now I submit along with Solomon to Allah, the Lord of the worlds.”
27|45|We sent to the people of Thamūd their brother Sālih [saying], “Worship Allah,” then they suddenly split into two quarreling factions
27|46|He said, “O my people, why do you seek to hasten punishment rather than good? If only you sought Allah’s forgiveness, so that you may be shown mercy!”
27|47|They said, “We consider you and those who are with you as a bad omen.” He said, “Your omen is from Allah, but you are a people who are being tested.”
27|48|There were nine men in the city who used to spread corruption in the land without doing anything good
27|49|They said, “Let us all swear by Allah that we will kill him and his family by night. Then we will tell his heir, ‘We did not witness the murder of his family, and we are indeed truthful.’”
27|50|Thus they made a plan and We too made a plan, but they were unaware of it
27|51|See then what was the consequences of their plan: We destroyed them and their entire people
27|52|Now their houses are utterly ruined because of their wrongdoing. Indeed, there are signs in this for people of knowledge
27|53|And We saved those who believed and feared Allah
27|54|And [remember] Lot, when he said to his people, “Do you commit this shameful act while seeing [one another]
27|55|Do you approach men with lust instead of women? In fact, you are an ignorant people!”
27|56|But the only response his people gave was to say, “Drive the family of Lot out of your town, for they are a people who keep themselves pure!”
27|57|So We saved him and his family, except his wife whom We destined to be among those who would remain behind
27|58|And We rained upon them a rain [of stones]. How terrible was the rain of those who were warned
27|59|Say, “All praise is for Allah, and peace be upon His slaves whom He has chosen. Is Allah better, or those partners whom they associate with Him?”
27|60|Is He [not better] Who created the heavens and earth, and sent down for you rain from the sky, by which We caused to grow gardens of cheerful beauty? You could never cause their trees to grow. Is there any god besides Allah? No, but they are people who ascribe equals [to Allah]
27|61|Is He [not better] Who made the earth a stable place to live, and caused rivers to flow through it, and placed therein firm mountains, and made a barrier between two flowing bodies of water? Is there any god besides Allah? No, but most of them do not know
27|62|Is He [not better] Who responds to the distressed when he calls out to Him, and Who relieves suffering, and Who makes you successors on earth? Is there any god besides Allah? Little is it that you take heed
27|63|Is He [not better] Who guides you in the depths of darkness of the land and sea, and Who sends the winds as harbingers ahead of His mercy? Is there any god besides Allah? Exalted is Allah far above the partners they associate with Him
27|64|Is He [not better] Who originates creation then repeats it, and Who gives you provision from the heaven and earth? Is there any god besides Allah? Say, “Produce your evidence if you are truthful.”
27|65|Say, “No one in the heavens and earth has knowledge of the unseen except Allah.” Nor do they know when they will be resurrected
27|66|In fact, their knowledge cannot comprehend the Hereafter; rather, they are in doubt about it; rather, they are blind to it
27|67|Those who disbelieve say, “What! Is it that when we and our forefathers become dust, will we really be brought forth [alive]
27|68|We and our forefathers have been promised this before; this is nothing but ancient fables!”
27|69|Say, “Travel in the land and see how was the end of the wicked.”
27|70|Do not grieve over them, nor be distressed by their plots
27|71|They say, “When will this warning come to pass, if you are truthful?”
27|72|Say, “Perhaps some of what you seek to hasten is quite near to you.”
27|73|Indeed, your Lord is graceful to mankind, but most of them are ungrateful
27|74|Your Lord surely knows all that their hearts conceal and all that they reveal
27|75|For there is nothing hidden in the heavens and earth except that it is [written] in a clear Record
27|76|Indeed, this Qur’an explains to the Children of Israel most of that over which they differ
27|77|And it is certainly a guidance and mercy for the believers
27|78|Indeed, your Lord will judge between them by His justice, for He is the All-Mighty, the All-Knowing
27|79|So put your trust in Allah, for you are upon the clear truth
27|80|You cannot make the dead hear, nor can you make the deaf hear the call when they turn their backs retreating
27|81|Nor can you guide the blind out of their error, nor can you make anyone hear except those who believe in Our verses, for they are ready to submit to Allah
27|82|When the decree [of the Hour] comes to pass against them, We will bring forth to them a beast out of the earth that will tell them that the people had no faith in Our verses
27|83|And [beware of] the Day when We will gather from every nation a group of those who used to reject Our verses, and they will be driven in ranks
27|84|When they finally come, He will say, “Did you reject My verses without even comprehending them, or what exactly were you doing
27|85|The decree [of punishment] will befall them because of their wrongdoing, leaving them speechless
27|86|Do they not see that We made the night for them to rest in, and made the day bright? Indeed, there are signs in this for people who believe
27|87|And [beware of] the Day when the Trumpet will be blown, and all those who are in the heavens and on earth will be horrified except whom Allah wills, and all will come to Him, fully humbled
27|88|You will see the mountains, thinking them firmly fixed, but they will be moving like clouds – such is the design of Allah, Who has perfected everything. Indeed, He is All-Aware of what you do
27|89|Whoever comes with a good deed will be rewarded with better than it, and they will be safe from the horror of that Day
27|90|But whoever comes with an evil deed will be thrown on their faces in the Fire. Are you recompensed except for what you used to do
27|91|Say, “I have been commanded only to worship the Lord of this city [of Makkah] Who made it sacred and to Whom belongs all things. And I am commanded to be one of those who submit to Allah [in Islam]
27|92|and to recite the Qur’an.” Then whoever chooses guidance, it is only for his own good; but whoever chooses to go astray, say [O Prophet], “I am only one of the warners.”
27|93|And say, “All praise is for Allah. He will show you His signs, then you will acknowledge them. Your Lord is not unaware of what you do.”
28|1|Tā Sīn Mīm
28|2|These are the verses of the clear Book
28|3|We recount to you part of the story of Moses and Pharaoh in truth for people who believe
28|4|Indeed, Pharaoh arrogantly elevated himself in the land and divided its people into different factions; oppressing one group of them, slaughtering their sons and sparing their women alive. He was truly one of those who spread corruption
28|5|But We wanted to bestow favor upon those who were oppressed in the land, and make them leaders and inheritors [of the land]
28|6|and to establish them in the land, and to show Pharaoh, Hamān and their soldiers that which they feared
28|7|We inspired the mother of Moses, “Suckle him; but when you fear for him, cast him into the river, and do not fear or grieve. We will surely return him to you, and will make him one of the messengers.”
28|8|Then the household of Pharaoh picked him up, so that he may become an enemy to them and a source of grief. Indeed, Pharaoh, Hāmān and their soldiers were wrongdoers
28|9|Pharaoh’s wife said, “He is a source of joy for me and you. Do not kill him; he will probably benefit us, or we may adopt him as a son.” They were unaware [of the consequences]
28|10|The heart of Moses’ mother became restless; she was about to disclose it, had We not reassured her heart so that she would maintain her faith [in Allah’s promise]
28|11|She said to his sister, “Keep track of him.” So she watched him from a distance, without them noticing
28|12|We had already forbidden for him all wet-nurses, then she said, “Shall I direct you to a household who will nurse him for you and take good care of him?”
28|13|Then We returned him to his mother, so that she would be comforted and not grieve, and so that she would know that Allah’s promise is true. Yet most of them do not know
28|14|When he reached his full strength and maturity, We gave him wisdom and knowledge. This is how We reward those who do good
28|15|Once he entered the city unnoticed by its people, and found two men fighting: one of his own people and the other of his enemies. The one from his own people called him for help against his enemy, so Moses struck him with his fist, causing his death. Moses said, “This is of Satan’s work; he is a sworn enemy who mislead people.”
28|16|He said, “My Lord, I have wronged myself, so forgive me,” Then He forgave him, for He is indeed the All-Forgiving, the Most Merciful
28|17|He said, “My Lord, because of the blessings that You have bestowed upon me, I will never be a supporter to the wicked.”
28|18|Then he became fearful and vigilant in the city; suddenly the one who sought his help the day before cried out to him again for help. Moses said to him, “You are clearly a troublemaker.”
28|19|When he was about to strike the one who was an enemy to both of them, he said, “O Moses, do you want to kill me as you killed that person yesterday? You only want to be a tyrant in the land, and you do not want to be one of those who put things right!”
28|20|Then there came a man rushing from the farthest end of the city, and said, “O Moses, the chiefs are conspiring to kill you, so leave. I am giving you a sincere advice.”
28|21|So he left the city, fearful and vigilant. He said, “My Lord, save me from the wrongdoing people.”
28|22|When he headed towards Midian, he said, “My Lord will surely guide me to a straight way.”
28|23|When he arrived at the well of Midian, he found a crowd of people watering [their flocks] and found apart from them two women holding [their flocks] back. He said, “What is the matter with you?” They said, “We cannot water [them] until the shepherds take [their flocks] away, and our father is a very old man.”
28|24|So he watered [their flocks] for them, then he turned to the shade and said, “My Lord, I am desperately in need of whatever good You may send down to me.”
28|25|Then one of the two women came to him, walking modestly. She said, “My father is inviting you so that he may reward you for watering [our flocks] for us.” When he came to him and told him the whole story, he said, “Have no fear. You are now safe from the wrongdoing people.”
28|26|One of the two daughters said, “O dear father, hire him; the best one you can hire is the strong and trustworthy.”
28|27|He said, “I would like to give you one of these two daughters of mine in marriage, provided that you serve me for eight years; if you complete ten, it will be of your own free will. I do not want to make things difficult for you. You will find me, if Allah wills, from among the righteous.”
28|28|Moses said, “Let that be the agreement between me and you. Whichever of the two terms I complete, there will be no further obligation on me, and Allah is Witness over what we say.”
28|29|When Moses had completed the term and was traveling with his family, he spotted a fire in the direction of Mount Tūr. He said to his family, “Stay here; I have spotted a fire. Perhaps I will bring you from there some news or a brand of fire so that you may warm yourselves.”
28|30|But when he came to it, he was called from the tree in the sacred ground on the right side of the valley: “O Moses, I am Allah, the Lord of the worlds
28|31|Throw down your staff.” But when he saw it slithering as if it were a snake, he turned and ran away without looking back. [Allah said], “O Moses, come back, and have no fear; you are perfectly safe
28|32|Put your hand into your garment, it will come out shining white without blemish; and draw your arms tight to you to calm your fear. These are two proofs from your Lord to Pharaoh and his chiefs, for they are indeed a rebellious people.”
28|33|Moses said, “My Lord, I have killed one of their men, and I fear that they may kill me
28|34|My brother Aaron is more eloquent than me in speech, so send him with me as a helper to confirm my words, for I fear that they may reject me.”
28|35|Allah said, “We will strengthen you through your brother and give you both power, so they cannot harm you. With Our signs, you and your followers will prevail.”
28|36|When Moses came to them with Our clear signs, they said, “This is nothing but fabricated magic; we have not heard of this from our earlier ancestors.”
28|37|Moses said, “My Lord knows best who has come with guidance from Him and who will have the best abode in the end. The wrongdoers will never succeed.”
28|38|Pharaoh said, “O chiefs, I do not know for you any god other than myself. So bake for me bricks out of clay, O Hāmān, and build for me a tower so that I may have a look at the God of Moses, for I think he is a liar.”
28|39|He and his soldiers were arrogant in the land without any right, and thought that they would not be brought back to Us
28|40|So We seized him and his soldiers and flung them into the sea. See how was the end of the wrongdoers
28|41|We made them leaders calling to the Fire, and on the Day of Resurrection they will not be helped
28|42|We caused a curse to pursue them in this world, and on the Day of Resurrection they will be among those who are despised
28|43|We gave Moses the Scripture after destroying earlier nations, as an insight for mankind, and a guidance and mercy, so that they may take heed
28|44|You were not [O Prophet] on the western side [of the mountain] when We gave Moses Our commandment, nor did you witness that event
28|45|But We brought forth many generations [after Moses], and a long time passed on them. And you [O Prophet] did not dwell among the people of Midian, rehearsing with them Our verses, but it is We Who sent you as a messenger [and revealed to you their stories]
28|46|You were not at the side of Mount Tūr when We called out [to Moses]. But [you have been sent] as a mercy from your Lord, to warn a people to whom no warner had come before you, so that they may take heed
28|47|So they would not say – if struck by a calamity because of what their hands have sent forth, “Our Lord, if only You had sent us a messenger, so we could follow Your verses and be among the believers?”
28|48|But when the truth came to them from Us, they said, “If only he was given the like of what was given to Moses before.” Did they not reject what was given to Moses before? They say, “Both [revelations] are works of magic, supporting each other”, adding, “We truly reject both of them.”
28|49|Say, “Then bring a scripture from Allah which is better in guidance than these two so that I may follow it, if you are truthful.”
28|50|But if they do not respond to you, then know that they only follow their desires. Who is more astray than one who follows his desire without any guidance from Allah? Indeed, Allah does not guide the wrongdoing people
28|51|Now We have conveyed Our Word to them, so that they may take heed
28|52|As for those whom We gave the Scripture before this [Qur’an], they do believe in it
28|53|When this [Qur’an] is recited to them, they say, “We believe in it, for it is the truth from our Lord. We had already submitted [as Muslims even] before this.”
28|54|They will be given their reward twice for their patience, repelling evil with good, and for spending out of what We have provided for them
28|55|When they hear vain talk, they turn away from it and say, “We are accountable for our deeds and you for yours. Peace [is our response] to you! We do not want [to be with] the ignorant.”
28|56|You cannot guide whoever you like, but Allah guides whom He wills, and He knows best who will be guided
28|57|They say, “If we follow the guidance with you [O Prophet], we will be snatched away from our land.” Have We not established for them a safe sanctuary [in Makkah] to which fruits of all kinds are brought as provision from Us? But most of them do not know
28|58|How many a town We have destroyed that were arrogant due to their affluence! Those are their dwellings which were never inhabited after them except briefly. It is We Who were the Inheritors
28|59|Your Lord would never destroy towns without first sending to their main city a messenger, reciting to them Our verses. Nor would We destroy towns unless their people were wrongdoers
28|60|Whatever you have been given is only an enjoyment and adornment of the life of this world, but what is with Allah is better and more lasting. Will you not then understand
28|61|Is one whom We promised a good promise – which he is going to obtain – like one whom We gave the pleasure of the life of this world, then on the Day of Resurrection he will be among those summoned [to Hellfire]
28|62|And [beware of] the Day when He will call out to them and say, “Where are those whom you claimed to be My partners?”
28|63|Those against whom the word will be fulfilled will say, “Our Lord, these are the ones whom we led astray; we led them astray as we ourselves went astray. We disassociate ourselves [from them] before You; it was not us that they used to worship.”
28|64|Then they will be told, “Call upon your [so-called] partners [for help].” They will call upon them, but will receive no response. They will see the punishment, wishing that they had followed guidance
28|65|On the Day when He will call out to them, saying, “What response did you give to the messengers?”
28|66|They will be dumbstruck on that Day, not even able to ask one another
28|67|But whoever repents and believes, and does righteous deeds, he will be among the successful
28|68|Your Lord creates and chooses what He wills; they have no choice. Glorified is Allah and Exalted is He far above what they associate with Him
28|69|Your Lord knows all that their hearts conceal and all that they reveal
28|70|He is Allah: none has the right to be worshiped except Him. All praise belongs to Him in this life and the Hereafter. His is the Judgment, and to Him you will all be returned
28|71|Say, “What do you think, if Allah were to make the night perpetual for you until the Day of Resurrection, which god other than Allah could bring you shining light? Do you not then listen?”
28|72|Say, “What do you think, if Allah were to make the day perpetual for you until the Day of Resurrection, which god other than Allah could bring you night to rest in? Do you not then see?”
28|73|It is out of His mercy that He made for you the night and day, so that you may rest therein and seek of His bounty, and so that you may be grateful
28|74|And [beware of] the Day when He will call out to them and say, “Where are those whom you claimed to be My partners?”
28|75|We will bring forth from every nation a witness and say, “Bring your proof.” They will then know that the truth is with Allah, and all [false gods] that they used to invent will be lost from them
28|76|Indeed, Korah was one of the people of Moses, but he behaved arrogantly towards them. We had given him such treasures that their keys would weigh down a group of strong men. When his people said to him, “Do not exult, for Allah does not like the exultant
28|77|Rather, seek with what Allah has given you the abode of the Hereafter, without forgetting your share of this world, and do good as Allah has done good to you, and do not seek to spread corruption in the land, for Allah does not like those who spread corruption.”
28|78|He said, “I have been given all this because of the knowledge that I have.” Did he not know that Allah destroyed some generations before him who were superior to him in power and greater in accumulating [wealth]? There will be no need for the wicked to be asked about their sins
28|79|He came out before his people in all his glamor. Those who desired the life of this world said, “Oh, would that we had the like of what Korah has been given! He is indeed a man of great fortune.”
28|80|But those who were given knowledge said, “Woe to you! Allah’s reward is better for those who believe and do righteous deeds. But none will attain this except those who are steadfast.”
28|81|Then We caused the earth to swallow him and his house. There was no one to help him against Allah, nor was he able to help himself
28|82|Those who had wished for his position the day before started saying, “Oh, it is surely Allah Who extends provisions to whom He wills or restricts it. If Allah had not favored us, He could have caused the earth to swallow us too. Oh, indeed the disbelievers will never succeed.”
28|83|That is the abode of the Hereafter We will assign to those who neither seek superiority nor corruption on earth. The best outcome is for those who fear Allah
28|84|Whoever comes with a good deed will be rewarded with what is better, and whoever comes with an evil deed, the evildoers will only be recompensed for what they used to do
28|85|Indeed, the One Who has ordained for you the Qur’an will bring you back home [to Makkah]. Say, “My Lord knows best who has come with guidance and who is clearly misguided.”
28|86|You were not expecting the Book to be revealed to you, but it was a mercy from your Lord. So never be a supporter to the disbelievers
28|87|Do not let them turn you away from Allah’s verses after they have been sent down to you. Rather, call people to your Lord, and never be among those who associate partners with Allah
28|88|Do not supplicate with Allah another god; none has the right to be worshiped except Him. Everything will perish except Him. His is the Judgment and to Him you will all be brought back
29|1|Alif Lām Mīm
29|2|Do people think once they say, “We believe,” that they will be left without being put to the test
29|3|We certainly tested those who came before them. For Allah will surely make known those who are truthful and those who are liars
29|4|Do the evildoers think that they can escape Us? How evil is their judgment
29|5|Whoever hopes to meet Allah, the time appointed by Allah is sure to come, and He is the All-Hearing, the All-Knowing
29|6|Whoever strives, he only strives for his own good. Indeed, Allah is in no need of the worlds
29|7|As for those who believe and do righteous deeds, We will surely expiate their sins, and reward them according to the best of what they used to do
29|8|We have enjoined upon man kindness to his parents. But if they strive to make you associate with Me what you have no knowledge of, then do not obey them. To Me is your return; then I will inform you of what you used to do
29|9|Those who believe and do righteous deeds, We will surely admit them among the righteous
29|10|There are some among people who say, “We believe in Allah”, but when they suffer for the sake of Allah, they deem the persecution of men as equal to the punishment of Allah. But when victory comes from your Lord, they will surely say, “We were with you.” Does Allah not know best what is in the hearts of all people
29|11|Allah will certainly make known those who truly believe and those who are hypocrites
29|12|Those who disbelieve say to those who believe, “Follow our way, and we will bear the burden of your sins.” But they will never bear any of their sins. They are indeed liars
29|13|They will certainly bear their own burdens, as well as other burdens along with their own burdens, and on the Day of Resurrection they will certainly be questioned concerning what they used to fabricate
29|14|We sent Noah to his people, and he lived among them for a thousand years, less fifty. Then the Flood overtook them, while they persisted in wrongdoing
29|15|But We saved him and those who were in the Ark, and We made it a sign for all people
29|16|And [remember] Abraham, when he said to his people, “Worship Allah and fear Him; that is better for you, if only you knew
29|17|You worship nothing besides Allah but idols and fabricate lies. Those whom you worship besides Allah have no power to give you provision. So seek provision from Allah, worship Him, and be grateful to Him. To Him you will all be returned
29|18|If you reject [the message], so did many nations reject before you. The duty of the Messenger is only to deliver the message clearly.”
29|19|Do they not see how Allah originates the creation then resurrects it? That is certainly easy for Allah
29|20|Say, “Travel through the land and see how He originated the creation, then Allah will repeat it a second time. Indeed, Allah is Most Capable of all things.”
29|21|He punishes whom He wills and shows mercy to whom He wills, and to Him you will all be returned
29|22|You cannot escape [His punishment] on earth or in the heaven, and you have no protector or helper besides Allah.”
29|23|Those who disbelieve in Allah’s signs and the meeting with Him, it is they who will have no hope in My mercy, and for them there will be a painful punishment
29|24|His people’s only response was to say, “Kill him or burn him!” But Allah saved him from the fire. Indeed, there are signs in this for people who believe
29|25|He said, “You have taken idols other than Allah as a means of love among yourselves in the life of this world, but on the Day of Resurrection you will disown and curse one another. Your abode will be the Fire, and you will have no helpers.”
29|26|Lot believed in him, and Abraham said, “I am emigrating to my Lord. He is indeed the All-Mighty, the All-Wise.”
29|27|We gave him Isaac and Jacob, and assigned prophethood and scripture to his offspring, and gave him his reward in this life, and in the Hereafter he will surely be among the righteous
29|28|And [remember] Lot, when he said to his people, “You surely commit a shameful act that no one in the world has ever done before you
29|29|Do you approach men with lust, engage in highway robbery, and practice immoral acts in your gatherings?” But the only response his people gave was to say, “Bring us Allah’s punishment, if you are truthful.”
29|30|He said, “My Lord, help me against people who spread corruption.”
29|31|When Our angel-messengers came to Abraham with glad tidings, they said, “We are going to destroy the people of this town, for its people have been persisting in wickedness.”
29|32|He said, “But Lot is there!” They said, “We know well who is there. We will surely save him and his family, except his wife; she is one of those who will remain behind.”
29|33|When Our angel-messengers came to Lot, he was distressed by their coming and felt troubled on their account, but they said, “Do not fear nor grieve; we will surely save you and your family, except your wife; she is one of those who will remain behind.”
29|34|We will surely send down on the people of this town a scourge from the heaven because of their evildoing.”
29|35|We surely left some of its ruins as a clear sign for people of understanding
29|36|To the people of Midian we sent their brother Shu‘ayb. He said, “O my people, worship Allah and expect the Last Day, and do not go about spreading corruption in the land.”
29|37|But they rejected him, so an earthquake seized them and they fell lifeless in their homes
29|38|And [We destroyed] ‘Ād and Thamūd, which is clear to you from their ruined dwellings. Satan made their deeds appealing to them and averted them from the right way, although they were a people of perception
29|39|And [We also destroyed] Korah, Pharaoh and Hāmān. Moses came to them with clear signs, but they showed arrogance in the land, yet they could not escape [Us]
29|40|Each of them We seized for their sin: against some of them We sent a storm of stones; some were seized by a blast; some We caused the earth to swallow; and some We drowned. It was not Allah Who wronged them, but it was they who wronged themselves
29|41|The likeness of those who take protectors other than Allah is that of a spider spinning a house. Indeed, the flimsiest of houses is the house of a spider, if only they knew
29|42|Allah knows whatever they call upon besides Him. He is the All-Mighty, the All-Wise
29|43|Such are the comparisons We set forth for people, but none will understand them except the people of knowledge
29|44|Allah created the heavens and earth for a true purpose. Indeed, there is a sign in this for the believers
29|45|Recite [O Prophet] what is revealed to you of the Book, and establish prayer, for indeed prayer restrains one from immoral acts and wickedness. Indeed, the remembrance of Allah is of greater merit. And Allah knows all what you do
29|46|Do not argue with the People of the Book except in the best manner, unless with those of them who transgress [against you]. And say, “We believe in what is sent down to us and what was sent down to you, and our God and your God is One, and to Him we submit.”
29|47|Thus We have sent down to you the Book. Those to whom We gave the Scripture believe in it, and from these [pagans] there are some who believe in it, and none rejects Our verses except the disbelievers
29|48|You [O Prophet] never recited any book before this, nor did you write with your hand. Otherwise, the people of falsehood would have raised suspicions
29|49|Rather, this [Qur’an] is clear verses [preserved] in the hearts of those who have been given knowledge. And none rejects Our verses except the wrongdoers
29|50|They say, “Why is it that no signs have been sent down to him from his Lord?” Say, “The signs are only with Allah, and I am only a clear warner.”
29|51|Is it not enough for them that We have sent down to you the Book which is being recited to them? Indeed, there is a mercy and reminder in it for people who believe
29|52|Say, “Allah is Sufficient as a Witness between me and you. He knows all that is in the heavens and earth. Those who believe in falsehood and disbelieve in Allah, it is they who are the losers.”
29|53|They ask you [O Prophet] to hasten the punishment. If it had not been for a time already set, the punishment would have come to them. But it will surely come to them by surprise when they least expect it
29|54|They ask you to hasten the punishment, but Hell will surely encompass the disbelievers
29|55|on the Day when the punishment will overwhelm them from above and from below their feet, and He will say, “Taste [the punishment] for what you used to do!”
29|56|O My believing slaves, My earth is spacious, so worship Me alone
29|57|Every soul will taste death, then to Us you will all be returned
29|58|As for those who believe and do righteous deeds, We will surely accommodate them in mansions of Paradise under which rivers flow, abiding therein forever. How excellent is the reward of those who work [righteousness]! –
29|59|those who endure patiently and put their trust in their Lord
29|60|How many creatures there are that cannot carry their provisions! It is Allah Who provides for them and for you, and He is the All-Hearing, the All-Knowing
29|61|If you ask them who created the heavens and earth and subjected the sun and moon, they will surely say, “Allah.” How are they then deluded
29|62|Allah extends provision to whom He wills of His slaves or restricts it. Indeed, Allah is All-Knowing of everything
29|63|If you ask them who sends down rain from the sky, then revives therewith the land after its death, they will surely say, “Allah”. Say, “All praise is for Allah,” but most of them do not understand
29|64|The life of this world is nothing but amusement and play, and the Abode of the Hereafter is indeed the real life, if only they knew
29|65|When they board a ship, they supplicate Allah, devoting their faith sincerely to Him. But as soon as He rescues them to the land, they associate partners with Him
29|66|showing their ingratitude to what We have given them and enjoy themselves, but they will soon come to know
29|67|Do they not see that We have made [Makkah] a safe sanctuary, while people around them are being snatched away? Do they still believe in falsehood and show ingratitude to Allah’s favors
29|68|Who does greater wrong than one who fabricates lies against Allah or rejects the truth when it comes to him? Is there not a home in Hell for the disbelievers
29|69|As for those who strive in Our cause, We will surely guide them to Our ways, for Allah is certainly with those who do good
30|1|Alif Lām Mīm
30|2|The Romans have been defeated
30|3|in a nearby land, but they will gain victory after their defeat
30|4|within a few years. To Allah belongs the whole matter before and after [the victory]. On that day the believers will rejoice
30|5|at the victory granted by Allah. He gives victory to whom He wills, and He is the All-Mighty, the Most Merciful
30|6|This is the promise of Allah. Allah never breaks His promise, but most people do not know
30|7|They only know the apparent life of this world, but they are heedless of the Hereafter
30|8|Do they not reflect on themselves? Allah did not create the heavens and earth and all that is between them except for a true purpose and for an appointed term, but most people deny the meeting with their Lord
30|9|Have they not traveled through the land to see how was the end of those who came before them? They were more powerful than them, and they tilled the land and built it more than these people have ever built. Their messengers came to them with clear proofs. It was not Allah Who wronged them, but it was they who wronged themselves
30|10|Then the end of the evildoers was utterly evil because they rejected the signs of Allah and used to ridicule them
30|11|Allah brings the creation into being, then He will repeat it, then to Him you will be returned
30|12|On the Day when the Hour begins, the wicked will be in utmost despair
30|13|They will have no intercessors among their [so-called] partners, rather they will disown those partners
30|14|On the Day when the Hour begins, the people will then be separated
30|15|As for those who believed and did righteous deeds, they will be rejoicing in a garden [of Paradise]
30|16|And as for those who disbelieved, and rejected Our signs and the meeting of the Hereafter, they will be arraigned for punishment
30|17|So glory be to Allah in the evening and in the morning
30|18|and all praise is due to Him in the heavens and earth – and [glorify Him] in the afternoon and at noon
30|19|He brings the living out of the dead and the dead out of the living, and gives life to the earth after its death. This is how you will be brought forth
